# Hive Registry UI — 对抗式 UX 审计报告

> 控件级重设计规格汇总。按共享原语、管理端页面、门户页面分组；末尾附 P0 全局清单。
> `重设计方案` 列保持原始规格原样（表格内的 `|` 以 `\|` 转义，渲染为字面竖线，不改变语义）。

## 1. 总览

| 维度 | 数量 |
|---|---|
| 审计对象总数 | 45 |
| &nbsp;&nbsp;— 共享原语 | 12 |
| &nbsp;&nbsp;— 管理端页面 | 20 |
| &nbsp;&nbsp;— 门户页面 | 13 |
| verdict = major | 45 |
| verdict = minor | 0 |
| verdict = ok | 0 |
| 控件级改动总数 | 498 |
| &nbsp;&nbsp;— P0 | 44 |
| &nbsp;&nbsp;— P1 | 172 |
| &nbsp;&nbsp;— P2 | 282 |

## 2. 共享原语改动（影响面最大）

> 这些原语被多页面复用，单点修复即全局收益；改动优先级整体高于单页。

### components/ui/data-table.tsx

- verdict: **major** · 控件数: 9 · P0/P1/P2: 2/4/3
- topPriority: Sortable column headers and clickable rows are entirely mouse-only — no tabIndex/role/onKeyDown/aria-sort on the sortable <th>, and onRowClick lives on a bare <tr> with cursor-pointer but no keyboard affordance. Since this is the only shared table primitive, every list view that uses sort or row-navigation is keyboard- and screen-reader-inaccessible. Fix these two before anything else.

| 控件 | 位置 | 严重度 | 反模式 | 重设计方案 |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Sortable column header (TableHead with onClick sort) | data-table.tsx:229-243 | P0 | Sort is wired via onClick on the <th> with cursor-pointer/hover styling, but there is no tabIndex, no role=button, no onKeyDown (Enter/Space), and no aria-sort attribute. Keyboard users cannot trigger a sort at all, and screen readers never announce that a column is sortable or its current asc/desc state — the ArrowUp/Down icons are decorative and uncommunicated. This is a hard a11y blocker inherited by every caller. | Wrap the header label+icon in a real <button type=button> (sort is an action, not a cell) so it is natively focusable and keyboard-activatable, OR add tabIndex=0 + role=button + onKeyDown handling Enter/Space to call getToggleSortingHandler(). Set aria-sort on the <th> to 'ascending'/'descending'/'none' from getIsSorted(). Give the sort control an aria-label like `Sort by {columnLabel}`. Mark the arrow icons aria-hidden. Add focus-visible ring matching the M3 token already used elsewhere. |
| Clickable row (onRowClick on <tr>) | data-table.tsx:264-271 | P0 | Row navigation is onClick on a <tr> with cursor-pointer but no tabIndex, no role, no keyboard handler, and no accessible name. In nodes.tsx this row click is the primary way to open node detail, so the whole drill-down is mouse-only and invisible to AT. Worse, stopPropagation is keyed off hardcoded column ids ('__select','actions') at line 273 — any other interactive content placed in a cell (a link, a Switch, a menu) will swallow into row navigation, a silent footgun for every future caller. | Prefer making the navigable cell content a real link/button (semantic, mid-table accessible) rather than a clickable row. If row-level click must stay, add role=button + tabIndex=0 + onKeyDown(Enter/Space) + an aria-label describing the destination, and a focus-visible ring. Replace the hardcoded interactive-column list with an explicit per-column flag (e.g. column.meta.stopRowClick) so callers opt in rather than relying on magic ids. |
| Search field | data-table.tsx:166-176 | P1 | onSearchChange fires on every keystroke with no debounce — nodes.tsx filters synchronously, but any caller that triggers a fetch will hammer the API. The input has only a placeholder (no <label>/aria-label), is not type=search, and has no clear (×) affordance, which M3 search fields require. There is also no `clearable`/`debounceMs` prop, so every caller would have to re-solve this. | Add an internal debounced wrapper (configurable `searchDebounceMs`, default ~250ms, with immediate clear). Render a visually-hidden <label> or aria-label on the Input, set type=search, and add a trailing clear button (icon, ≥48dp hit area, aria-label='Clear search') shown when searchValue is non-empty. Expose `clearable` and `searchDebounceMs` props. |
| Loading state | data-table.tsx:249-256 | P1 | Loading swaps the entire body for a bare spinner div with no role=status, no aria-live, and no accessible text — screen readers announce nothing while data loads. Existing rows are fully replaced (content disappears) instead of a skeleton, and search/sort/pagination stay interactive over stale state. Only a binary `loading` prop exists; no skeleton vs spinner choice. | Wrap the loading indicator with role=status + aria-live=polite and a visually-hidden 'Loading…' label. Prefer skeleton rows that preserve column count/width over a body-wide spinner to avoid layout shift; offer a `loadingVariant: 'skeleton'\|'spinner'` prop. When reloading with data already present, overlay/dim rather than blanking. Consider disabling sort/search interactions while loading. |
| Pagination controls | data-table.tsx:293-320 | P1 | The four nav buttons are forced to h-9 w-9 (36px), below the M3 48dp touch-target minimum, making them hard to hit on mobile. There is no rows-per-page selector and no range readout ('1–20 of 100') — just total 'X rows'; the page-size is locked at mount via initialState so changing the `pageSize` prop later has no effect. The whole pager is hidden when pageCount<=1, so total count vanishes for short lists. Buttons also lack aria-labels (icon-only) and the pager has no nav landmark. | Restore ≥48dp targets (use size='icon' = 40px minimum, ideally icon-lg / expanded hit area) and add aria-label to each (First/Previous/Next/Last page). Wrap in <nav aria-label='Pagination'>. Show a range indicator and an optional rows-per-page Select (expose `pageSizeOptions`). Drive page size from a reactive state, not initialState only. Add `manualPagination`/`pageCount`/`totalCount` props for server-side paging since the client-only model renders all rows. |
| Selection checkboxes + select-all | data-table.tsx:105-126,146-151 | P1 | The header checkbox is aria-label='Select all' but only calls toggleAllPageRowsSelected — it selects the current page, not all data, which is misleading across multi-page tables; it also never reflects an indeterminate (some-selected) state. Row/header checkboxes in dense rows have no enlarged hit area (<48dp touch target). onSelectionChange runs in a useEffect keyed only on rowSelection with exhaustive-deps disabled, risking stale callbacks. | Label the header checkbox 'Select all on this page' (or implement true select-all-across-pages) and set indeterminate from getIsSomePageRowsSelected(). Expand checkbox hit area to ≥48dp (padding/pseudo-target) without changing visual size. Notify selection via TanStack's onRowSelectionChange callback path rather than a deps-suppressed effect. |
| Batch-actions bar | data-table.tsx:207-216 | P2 | The 'N selected' bar appears with no role=region/aria-live, so screen readers are not told the count changed or that batch actions became available. There is also no 'Clear selection' affordance inside the bar, and the bar carries the destructive/bulk actions (enable/disable in nodes.tsx) but the primitive provides no confirmation hook for destructive batchActions — confirmation is left entirely to each caller. | Give the bar role=region + aria-live=polite + aria-label so the selection count is announced. Add a built-in 'Clear' button (expose onClearSelection) and an aria-label. Document/encourage a confirmation pattern for destructive batch actions, or accept a `confirmBatch` render slot so destructive bulk ops are consistently guarded. |
| Empty state | data-table.tsx:257-262 | P2 | Empty state is a single line of muted text with no icon, no guidance, and no CTA. The filtered-vs-empty branch keys only on searchValue.trim(), so when a toolbar filter (e.g. the status tabs in nodes.tsx) yields zero rows but search is blank, the generic 'no data' message shows even though results were filtered out — confusing and offers no 'clear filters' path. | Render a proper empty-state block (icon + title + supporting text + optional action slot). Add an `isFiltered` prop (or accept a filtered-row signal) so the filtered message is shown whenever ANY filter is active, not just search, and surface a 'Clear filters' action. Expose an `emptyAction`/`renderEmpty` slot for reuse. |
| Table semantics, motion & density | data-table.tsx:219-290 | P2 | The table has no accessible name (no caption/aria-label), so AT announces an unlabeled table. Every row gets animate-slide-up with a staggered animationDelay (line 269) that re-fires on every sort/filter/page change, producing repeated motion with no prefers-reduced-motion guard (vestibular concern). The primitive also lacks reusability props common to a shared table: row density/`size` (compact vs comfortable), sticky header, and per-column alignment — forcing visual hacks per caller. | Add an `ariaLabel`/`caption` prop applied to the <table>. Gate the entrance animation behind prefers-reduced-motion (and ideally only animate on initial mount, not on every re-sort/paginate). Add a `size`/`density` prop driving row padding and header height to keep touch targets ≥48dp in comfortable mode while allowing compact, plus an optional `stickyHeader`. |

### components/ui/select.tsx

- verdict: **major** · 控件数: 10 · P0/P1/P2: 0/4/6
- topPriority: Touch targets are sub-spec everywhere: SelectTrigger is h-9 (36px) default / h-8 (32px) sm, and SelectItem rows are py-2 (~36px). M3 requires ≥48dp interactive targets. Because this is the shared select, every filter dropdown across all 8 pages is undersized on touch — fix the trigger size scale and item height first.

| 控件 | 位置 | 严重度 | 反模式 | 重设计方案 |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| SelectTrigger | components/ui/select.tsx:27-51 (data-[size=default]:h-9, data-[size=sm]:h-8) | P1 | Trigger heights are 36px (default) and 32px (sm). Both are below the M3 minimum 48dp touch target, and there is no size that reaches it. On a touch device every status/filter dropdown is hard to hit. | Introduce a 3-step size scale: sm=h-9 (36px, dense desktop tables only), default=h-10 (40px), lg=h-12 (48px touch-compliant). Keep the visible control at its design height but guarantee a ≥48px hit area on coarse pointers via a pseudo-element or min-h on coarse-pointer media (e.g. `@media (pointer:coarse)` → min-h-12). Default size should map to the same height as Input for visual parity across forms. |
| SelectItem | components/ui/select.tsx:103-128 (py-2 ... pl-2.5 pr-8) | P1 | Menu rows are py-2 text-sm (~36px tall). M3 list/menu items should be ≥48dp for touch. Long status lists (orders has 5 options) are cramped and mis-tap-prone on mobile. | Raise item min height to 48px on coarse pointers (min-h-12) while allowing a compact 40px on fine pointers, mirroring the trigger size scale. Tie item density to the parent size via a context/data attribute so a `lg` trigger yields `lg` items rather than every item being a fixed height. |
| Select (root) — async/loading | components/ui/select.tsx:9-13; evidence: pages/gateway.tsx:38-92 hand-rolls Popover+Command | P1 | No `loading` affordance. Selects fed by async data (customers, nodes, users) show an empty or stale dropdown while fetching, with no skeleton/spinner. gateway.tsx had to abandon this primitive entirely and build a Popover+Command for the async/searchable case. | Add a `loading?: boolean` prop on SelectTrigger that swaps the chevron for a spinner and sets aria-busy, plus a `loading` slot in SelectContent that renders a spinner row instead of items. Provide a documented pattern so consumers stop hand-rolling. |
| Select — searchable / long lists | components/ui/select.tsx (whole); evidence: pages/gateway.tsx uses Command instead | P1 | No filter/search support. For long option sets (customers, nodes) users must scroll a plain list. gateway.tsx proves the gap by reaching for Popover+Command, fragmenting the select pattern across the app. | Either add an optional `searchable` mode (a sticky Command-style input inside SelectContent that filters SelectItems) or formally document that long/searchable selects use the existing Combobox/Command primitive — and align the two visually. Pick one canonical control per use case so consumers stop diverging. |
| SelectValue / clearable | components/ui/select.tsx:21-25; evidence: orders.tsx:204 & tickets.tsx:122 use value="all" sentinel | P2 | No `clearable` affordance. Once a value is picked there is no way to return to the unset/placeholder state, so every consumer invents a fake `value="all"` sentinel item to mean 'no filter'. That leaks filter semantics into the option list and can't represent a truly empty selection. | Add an optional `clearable` prop on SelectTrigger that renders a small clear (X) button when a value is set, calling onValueChange('' or undefined). Keep it ≥24px and inside the 48dp target. This removes the need for sentinel options. |
| SelectContent — empty state | components/ui/select.tsx:53-88 | P2 | When there are zero items (async list resolved empty), the dropdown opens as a tiny empty box with no message. Users can't tell if it's loading, broken, or genuinely empty. | Add an `emptyLabel`/empty slot rendered when no SelectItems are present (e.g. 'No options'), centered and muted, with min-h to avoid a collapsed popover. |
| SelectTrigger — default width | components/ui/select.tsx:40 (w-fit); evidence: tickets.tsx:117 w-40, orders.tsx:200 w-44 | P2 | Trigger defaults to `w-fit`, so width jumps as the selected label changes (layout shift), and every consumer must override with w-40/w-44. Inconsistent widths across filters and shifting toolbars. | Default to a stable width (e.g. w-full within a sized container, or a min-w token) and document a width convention. Avoid w-fit as the default since it guarantees reflow on value change. |
| SelectContent — positioning on mobile | components/ui/select.tsx:56 (position default 'item-aligned') | P2 | Default position is overridden to 'item-aligned' (Radix default is 'popper'). item-aligned can position the selected item over the trigger and overflow small viewports, and it ignores trigger-width var — worse mobile reachability than popper. | Default to position='popper' with side/align collision handling and `min-w-[var(--radix-select-trigger-width)]` so the menu tracks the trigger and stays on-screen on mobile. Allow item-aligned opt-in for the rare long-static-list case. |
| SelectTrigger / SelectValue — ARIA error + label wiring | components/ui/select.tsx:40 (aria-invalid styling) & :21-25 | P2 | aria-invalid styling exists but there is no built-in error-message wiring (aria-describedby) and no required indication. Label association is left entirely to each consumer, so screen-reader users get the invalid border styling with no announced reason. | Accept optional `error`/`errorId` and wire aria-describedby + aria-invalid on the trigger automatically; expose a documented Label+id pairing. Surface required state to AT. Keep this opt-in so non-form filter selects are unaffected. |
| SelectScrollUp/DownButton — affordance | components/ui/select.tsx:143-177 (py-1, cursor-default) | P2 | Scroll buttons are py-1 (~24px) and cursor-default — too small to tap on touch and visually undistinguished from items, so users may not realize the list scrolls. | Increase scroll-button hit area to ≥40px on coarse pointers and give a subtle gradient/elevation cue that more items exist. Lower priority since popper+native scroll covers most cases once positioning is fixed. |

### components/ui/switch.tsx

- verdict: **major** · 控件数: 5 · P0/P1/P2: 0/3/2
- topPriority: Hit area equals the tiny visual track (default 32×18.4px, sm 24×14px) with zero inset expansion — every Switch on every page fails the M3 ≥48dp touch target. Add an invisible ≥48dp hit overlay (padding/::before) decoupled from the visual track so the control is enlarged once, for all callers, without changing the finalized visuals.

| 控件 | 位置 | 严重度 | 反模式 | 重设计方案 |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Switch (root touch target) | components/ui/switch.tsx:19-27 (data-[size=default]:h-[1.15rem] w-8 / data-[size=sm]:h-3.5 w-6) | P1 | The Radix Root is both the visual track AND the only clickable element. Default renders ~32×18.4px, sm ~24×14px. There is no inset hit-area expansion (no negative-margin ::before, no min-h/min-w, no padding). Pointer/tap target is identical to the visual pill, far below M3's 48dp minimum. On the gateway table and announcement form this is a thumb-sized tap target on mobile. | Keep the visual track sizes finalized, but decouple the interactive target. Wrap or layer a transparent hit region: add a `::before` with `absolute inset-[-15px]` (default) / `inset-[-17px]` (sm) and `content-['']`, or render the visual track inside a Root that has `min-h-[48px] min-w-[48px] grid place-items-center` with the colored pill as a child span. Net: visual unchanged, tappable area ≥48×48dp everywhere. |
| Switch (async / loading semantics) | components/ui/switch.tsx:8-14 (props) consumed by pages/gateway.tsx:387-392 onCheckedChange -> onPatch network call | P1 | No `loading`/`pending` prop. gateway.tsx flips the switch and fires an async PATCH (gateway_enabled) immediately; the only in-flight protection is an externally-managed `rowDisabled`. While the request is in flight there is no built-in feedback, no aria-busy, and nothing prevents the optimistic thumb from visually contradicting server state or being double-toggled. Each consumer must reinvent disable+spinner wiring. | Add `loading?: boolean`. When true: set `aria-busy`, force `disabled` (block re-toggle), and render a small spinner/progress affordance in the thumb (M3 switch supports a thumb indicator) instead of leaving the thumb static. Optionally expose `onCheckedChange` returning a Promise so the primitive can own the pending window. Removes the per-caller disable-juggling currently in gateway.tsx. |
| Switch (accessible name / label association) | components/ui/switch.tsx (no id/label API) vs pages/announcements.tsx:385-389,392-395 (adjacent <Label> with no htmlFor) | P1 | The primitive neither requires nor wires an accessible name. gateway.tsx happens to pass aria-label, but announcements.tsx renders <Switch> next to a plain <Label> with no `id`/`htmlFor` linkage — the switch has NO accessible name for screen readers, and clicking the visible label does not toggle it (lost tap target, compounding the touch-size issue). | Provide a labeled composition contract: either ship a `SwitchField`/`label` prop that auto-generates an `id` and renders an associated <Label htmlFor>, or document+lint that every Switch needs `aria-label`/`aria-labelledby`. At minimum default an internal `id` so callers can wire a clickable label. Fix announcements.tsx to associate its labels so the label is part of the toggle target. |
| Switch (size scale) | components/ui/switch.tsx:12-14,23 (size?: 'sm' \| 'default') | P2 | Only two sizes, both below tappable size, and no responsive growth on coarse pointers. There is no way for a touch-dense surface (mobile portal) to opt into a larger visual switch; the only knob shrinks it further (sm), worsening reachability. | Once the hit area is decoupled (P1#1), keep sm/default visuals but add a `lg` visual variant and/or grow the visual track under `@media (pointer: coarse)`. Discourage `sm` outside dense desktop tables; note in DESIGN_SYSTEM that sm must still carry the full 48dp hit overlay. |
| Switch (state conveyed by color only) | components/ui/switch.tsx:30-37 (thumb: color + position only) | P2 | On/off is communicated purely by track color and thumb position/color. M3 switches support an optional thumb icon (check/blank) precisely so state is not color-only — relevant for color-vision-deficient users and small sm size where the 2px travel is hard to perceive. | Add an optional `showIcon` (default true per M3) rendering a check glyph in the checked thumb and nothing/none when unchecked, sized to the thumb. Reinforces state non-chromatically without altering the finalized palette. |

### components/ui/dialog.tsx

- verdict: **major** · 控件数: 11 · P0/P1/P2: 3/4/4
- topPriority: No AlertDialog variant for destructive confirmation: all delete flows (plans/users/customers/orders/etc.) hand-roll a plain Dialog with a duplicated spinner SVG and ad-hoc error-colored button, getting role="dialog" instead of role="alertdialog", no enforced Cancel-first focus, and a primitive that closes on Escape/outside-click even mid-request. Add an AlertDialog primitive (or destructive mode) with a built-in loading prop and non-dismissible-while-pending behavior.

| 控件 | 位置 | 严重度 | 反模式 | 重设计方案 |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| AlertDialog / destructive-confirm variant | dialog.tsx — entire file (no alertdialog export); callers e.g. pages/plans.tsx:454-489, customers/[id].tsx, orders.tsx, users.tsx, lines.tsx | P0 | There is no AlertDialog primitive. Every destructive confirmation reuses the generic Dialog, so the dialog announces as role="dialog" not role="alertdialog", does not force initial focus onto the safe (Cancel) action, and each page re-implements an inline animate-spin SVG + bg-md-error button + `disabled={deleting}` (plans.tsx:475-486 duplicated verbatim across ~6 pages). Confirmation semantics, focus order, and busy state are decided per-caller instead of by the shared control. | Export AlertDialog/AlertDialogContent/AlertDialogAction/AlertDialogCancel wrapping radix-ui AlertDialog (role=alertdialog, focus defaults to Cancel). Give AlertDialogAction a `loading` boolean that renders the shared Spinner, sets aria-busy, and disables the button; and a `destructive` style hook mapping to bg-md-error/md-on-error. This removes the copy-pasted SVG and standardizes confirm UX. |
| DialogContent — pending/async dismissal guard | dialog.tsx:50-82 | P0 | DialogContent forwards no controlled props for dismissal, so while an async delete/save is in flight (`deleting`/`saving` true) the user can still press Escape or click the overlay and dismiss the dialog — the request keeps running but the UI unmounts, orphaning the spinner/feedback and risking a state desync. The X close button also stays interactive during pending state. | Add a `dismissible`/`pending` prop on DialogContent that, when pending, wires onEscapeKeyDown/onPointerDownOutside/onInteractOutside to preventDefault and disables the close button. Default keeps current behavior; destructive/submit flows pass pending to lock the surface until the operation resolves. |
| DialogDescription wiring (aria-describedby) | dialog.tsx:50-82 (Content) & 134-145 (Description); 22 DialogContent usages, 0 DialogDescription usages in pages/ | P0 | DialogDescription is exported but used 0 times across all 22 DialogContent call sites, and DialogContent neither renders a description slot nor passes `aria-describedby={undefined}`. Radix therefore emits a runtime a11y warning for every dialog and, more importantly, screen-reader users get a title with no described context for the dialog body. Body copy is placed in raw <p> tags (plans.tsx:460) that are never associated to the dialog. | Either (a) accept an optional `description` prop on DialogContent that renders a DialogDescription with a generated id and sets aria-describedby, or (b) pass aria-describedby={undefined} explicitly when no description is provided to suppress the warning. Update call sites to pass real description text so confirmation/forms are announced. |
| Close button touch target | dialog.tsx:71-77 | P1 | The X close button is `size-8` (32px) with a `size-4` (16px) icon. M3 requires interactive targets ≥48dp; 32px fails on touch and sits in the top-right corner where thumb reach is poor on mobile. It is the only persistent dismiss affordance. | Bump the hit area to min 44-48px: use `size-10`/`size-11` or wrap a 40px visual chip in a 48px tap target via padding, keeping the icon at 20px (size-5 per M3 icon-button). Preserve the state-layer and focus ring. |
| DialogContent — scroll / overflow handling | dialog.tsx:61-68 | P1 | DialogContent is `grid gap-4 ... p-6` with no max-height or internal overflow. Long forms (customers, orders, plans line-editor) exceed the viewport on mobile/short screens; the header and footer actions scroll off-screen with the page, so Save/Cancel can become unreachable. Callers patch this ad hoc (plans.tsx:505 wraps one inner list in max-h-64), but the dialog body itself never scrolls. | Constrain DialogContent to `max-h-[calc(100dvh-2rem)]` and make it a flex column with a scrollable body region between a sticky DialogHeader and sticky DialogFooter, so title and actions stay pinned while only the body scrolls. This is the single biggest mobile-reachability fix and benefits every form dialog. |
| size prop | dialog.tsx:61-66 (hardcoded sm:max-w-lg) | P1 | Max width is hardcoded `max-w-[calc(100%-2rem)] sm:max-w-lg`. Every caller that needs a different width overrides via className (customers.tsx:345 max-w-md, :409 max-w-sm, plans.tsx duplicates p-0 gap-0 layout). There is no size contract, so widths drift (sm/md/lg) inconsistently across pages. | Add a `size?: 'sm'\|'md'\|'lg'\|'xl'` prop mapping to fixed max-widths, defaulting to current lg. Removes per-page className width hacks and standardizes the dialog scale. |
| DialogFooter — action layout & primary semantics | dialog.tsx:94-119; callers plans.tsx:464-488 | P1 | DialogFooter only lays out children (`flex-col-reverse ... sm:justify-end`) and offers a generic showCloseButton. It encodes no notion of primary vs secondary/destructive action, so every caller hand-builds two raw <button> elements with full Tailwind class strings (plans.tsx:464-488) instead of using the Button primitive — inconsistent focus rings, loading states, and ordering across pages. | Provide a structured footer API (or document that footers must use the Button primitive) with explicit primary/cancel slots; pair with AlertDialogAction/Cancel. On mobile keep full-width stacked buttons (≥48dp height) with the confirming action ordered per platform convention. Eliminates raw-button duplication. |
| Initial focus control | dialog.tsx:50-82 (no onOpenAutoFocus / initialFocus support) | P2 | DialogContent exposes no helper for initial focus. For form dialogs focus should land on the first field; for destructive confirms it should land on Cancel, not the destructive button or the close X. Today focus defaults to the first tabbable (often the close X), which is suboptimal and unsafe for delete flows. | Expose/forward onOpenAutoFocus (Radix already supports it) and document an `initialFocus` ref pattern; have the AlertDialog variant default focus to Cancel. Keeps keyboard users from landing on a destructive control. |
| Inline submit loading state | dialog.tsx (none); plans.tsx:286 saving disable, :479-486 spinner SVG | P2 | Form submit buttons inside dialogs duplicate the same animate-spin SVG and `disabled={saving\|\|!formName.trim()}` logic (plans.tsx:286, :475). The dialog/button layer offers no loading affordance, so busy feedback is reinvented and visually inconsistent per page. | Once Button (or AlertDialogAction) gains a shared `loading` prop, dialog submit/confirm buttons consume it instead of inlining SVGs. Centralizes aria-busy + disabled + spinner. |
| Open animation symmetry | dialog.tsx:64 | P2 | Content uses a custom `animate-scale-in` for entry but the exit relies on radix data-[state=closed]:zoom-out-95/fade-out-0; there is no matching data-[state=open] enter from the standard radix set. Several callers also re-declare animate-scale-in in className (plans.tsx:203), indicating the base animation isn't trusted/consistent. | Define open/close transitions purely via data-[state=open]/[state=closed] utilities on the base component so callers never re-pass animation classes, ensuring symmetric enter/exit and removing duplicated className animation. |
| DialogHeader/Footer alignment defaults | dialog.tsx:84-92, 94-119 | P2 | DialogHeader defaults to `text-center sm:text-left`, which suits an alert/confirm but reads oddly for standard form dialogs where left-aligned titles are expected; callers override per page, and there's no variant signal tying centered headers to alert usage. | Default header to left-aligned for the generic Dialog and reserve centered text for the AlertDialog variant, so alignment communicates dialog type instead of being a per-caller override. |

### components/ui/command.tsx

- verdict: **major** · 控件数: 8 · P0/P1/P2: 1/4/3
- topPriority: CommandDialog renders DialogTitle/DialogDescription OUTSIDE DialogContent, so every command palette opens with no accessible name and Radix throws its missing-title warning. Fix the nesting (move DialogHeader inside DialogContent) — this is a one-line structural correction that affects every future palette consumer.

| 控件 | 位置 | 严重度 | 反模式 | 重设计方案 |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| CommandDialog | components/ui/command.tsx:43-58 | P0 | DialogHeader (containing the sr-only DialogTitle + DialogDescription) is rendered as a SIBLING before DialogContent, not as a descendant of it. Radix Dialog wires aria-labelledby/aria-describedby by locating DialogTitle/Description INSIDE the content node. As written the content has no Title descendant: the modal opens with no accessible name, screen readers announce only 'dialog', and Radix emits its console warning 'DialogContent requires a DialogTitle'. Every consumer of this palette inherits the defect. | Move the DialogHeader (sr-only Title/Description) INSIDE DialogContent, above the Command. Keep it visually hidden but in the accessibility tree. Confirm Radix no longer warns. Optionally expose aria-describedby wiring so the description is announced. |
| CommandItem | components/ui/command.tsx:140-154 | P1 | Base item height is px-3 py-2.5 (~40px) — below the M3 48dp touch target. The CommandDialog wrapper patches items to py-3 via a [&_[cmdk-item]]:py-3 override, but ANY consumer that uses Command directly (e.g. location-combobox at location-combobox.tsx:59-66) gets the 40px version. Also uses cursor-default on a clickable/selectable row, weakening mouse affordance. | Make the base CommandItem itself meet >=48dp (min-h-12 / py-3) so density is correct without per-consumer overrides; add an optional size prop ('default' 48dp touch \| 'compact' for dense admin lists) instead of the dialog re-patching geometry. Switch cursor-default to cursor-pointer for pointer users. |
| CommandList / CommandEmpty | components/ui/command.tsx:83-109 | P1 | No loading state. cmdk filters client-side, so during async option fetching (location-combobox feeds a large remote list) the list is empty and CommandEmpty immediately renders '无匹配结果 / no results' — a false negative that reads as 'nothing exists' while data is still loading. There is also no distinction between 'haven't typed yet', 'loading', and 'genuinely empty'. | Add a CommandLoading slot (cmdk exposes Command.Loading) and a loading prop on the primitive; render a spinner/skeleton row while pending and suppress CommandEmpty until loading resolves. Provide a distinct initial-idle vs empty-after-search message hook. |
| CommandEmpty | components/ui/command.tsx:99-109 | P1 | The empty/results state is not announced. CommandEmpty is a plain div with no aria-live region, so when filtering dynamically removes all matches (or results count changes) screen-reader users get no feedback — they keep typing into apparent silence. Violates the ARIA combobox/listbox feedback expectation. | Wrap the empty message (and ideally a live result count) in an aria-live='polite' region with role='status' so result/empty transitions are announced. Keep it inside the listbox structure cmdk manages. |
| CommandInput | components/ui/command.tsx:61-81 | P1 | No clearable affordance and no enforced accessible label. The search field exposes only a placeholder ('搜索...' in location-combobox), and placeholder is not an accessible name — once text is typed the field is effectively unlabeled. There is also no trailing clear (X) button, so on touch a user must backspace the whole query; the leading search icon is decorative but lacks aria-hidden. | Require/forward an aria-label (or label association) rather than relying on placeholder. Add an optional clearable prop rendering a >=48dp trailing icon-button (with sr-only 'clear search') that resets the value via onValueChange. Mark the leading SearchIcon aria-hidden. Optionally add debounce/onValueChange guidance for server-side search (shouldFilter=false) since consumers currently must wire this manually. |
| CommandList | components/ui/command.tsx:83-97 | P2 | max-h-[320px] is hard-coded with no override prop and no virtualization. location-combobox can render large administrative-division lists (all provinces/cities) as one flat CommandGroup; long unvirtualized lists hurt scroll/keyboard performance and the fixed 320px isn't responsive to small viewports. | Expose a height/maxHeight prop (or allow className to win predictably), document a virtualization path for large option sets, and consider grouping long lists. On mobile, cap to viewport-relative height. |
| CommandShortcut | components/ui/command.tsx:156-170 | P2 | Shortcut hint is a bare span with no semantics. Screen readers read the raw glyphs (e.g. '⌘K') out of context, and there is no association with the action it triggers. | Add aria-hidden by default (the shortcut is a visual hint) or, when it should be announced, provide an aria-label like 'shortcut: Ctrl K'. Make it a controlled prop rather than implicit. |
| CommandDialog (dead/duplicated geometry selectors) | components/ui/command.tsx:53 | P2 | The Command className targets cmdk-input-wrapper and cmdk-input attributes, but CommandInput emits data-slot='command-input-wrapper' / 'command-input' (custom div), not those raw cmdk attributes. Several of these descendant selectors are dead, and they duplicate sizing already set in CommandInput — geometry now lives in two places and drifts (input wrapper h-14 here vs h-12 in CommandInput). | Drive density from the CommandInput/CommandItem primitives (via a size prop) and delete the stale cmdk-* override selectors so there is a single source of truth for touch-target geometry. |

### components/ui/dropdown-menu.tsx

- verdict: **major** · 控件数: 7 · P0/P1/P2: 2/3/2
- topPriority: P0: every interactive item (Item/CheckboxItem/RadioItem/SubTrigger) is ~36px tall (py-2 + text-sm), below the M3 48dp touch target. This is a primitive used for destructive row actions on a data table — the most touch-sensitive surface — so the undersizing ships to every consumer at once. Add a `size` prop defaulting to a 48dp-compliant min-height and bump default item padding.

| 控件 | 位置 | 严重度 | 反模式 | 重设计方案 |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| DropdownMenuItem / CheckboxItem / RadioItem / SubTrigger — touch target height | dropdown-menu.tsx:75 (Item), :93 (Checkbox), :129 (Radio), :212 (SubTrigger) | P0 | All four interactive item types use `px-2.5 py-2 text-sm` → 8px top/bottom padding + ~20px line-height ≈ 36px row height. M3 mandates ≥48dp pointer targets. On nodes.tsx the dropdown holds View + Delete (destructive) actions hit by finger on mobile; data-table column-toggle checkboxes are even smaller-feeling because the indicator sits in a 14px box. No way for a consumer to opt into a comfortable size. | Add a `size?: 'sm' \| 'default' \| 'comfortable'` prop (or a CVA variant) to the item family. `comfortable` (mobile default) → `min-h-12 py-2.5`; `default` (dense desktop menus) → `min-h-9`. Set the family default to enforce `min-h-9` at minimum and `min-h-12` under a coarse-pointer media query (`pointer-coarse:min-h-12`). Apply identically to CheckboxItem/RadioItem/SubTrigger so checked-state and submenu rows match. |
| DropdownMenuItem — destructive confirmation semantics | dropdown-menu.tsx:60-81 + consumer pages/nodes.tsx:165 (window.confirm) / :251 delete item | P0 | The primitive exposes `variant="destructive"` purely as a color token; it carries no interaction contract. The only consumer wires destructive delete to a native `window.confirm()` (nodes.tsx:166,178). A destructive menu item that fires immediately on select/Enter with only a browser-native confirm is inconsistent with the app's own Dialog primitive and is easy for other consumers to copy without any confirm at all. Nothing in the primitive nudges callers toward a guarded flow. | Keep `variant="destructive"` for styling but document/enforce a guarded pattern: either expose a `confirm?: { title; description; confirmLabel }` prop that internally renders the AlertDialog/Dialog primitive on select (preventing default close), or ship a `DropdownMenuDestructiveItem` wrapper that requires a confirm handler. At minimum, destructive items should not auto-dismiss the menu before confirmation resolves. Replace window.confirm usage in nodes.tsx with the dialog primitive. |
| DropdownMenuItem — cursor + clickability affordance | dropdown-menu.tsx:75 (`cursor-default`), :93, :129, :212 | P1 | Every interactive item hardcodes `cursor-default`, signalling non-clickable. Consumers are forced to override with `cursor-pointer` (nodes.tsx:251 does exactly this on the delete item, but the View item at :244 does NOT — so within one menu one row shows a pointer and the other an arrow). The primitive's default actively fights its own purpose and creates inconsistency. | Default actionable items to `cursor-pointer`. Reserve `cursor-default` only for non-actionable labels (DropdownMenuLabel already is non-interactive, so it's safe). Removing the override burden also eliminates the nodes.tsx inconsistency automatically. |
| DropdownMenu family — no loading / async-pending state | dropdown-menu.tsx:60-81 (Item), whole file | P1 | Items have no `loading` / `pending` affordance. Real consumers run async work on select (nodes.tsx delete → API; batchAction → API). On a slow network the menu closes instantly and the user gets no in-menu feedback that the action is in flight; double-activation is possible before the row disappears. No spinner slot, no `disabled`-while-pending wiring. | Add `loading?: boolean` to DropdownMenuItem: when true, render a leading spinner (reuse the app spinner), set `aria-disabled`/`data-disabled`, and block re-selection. Optionally expose `closeOnSelect?: boolean` (default true) so async items can keep the menu open until the promise resolves, then close programmatically. |
| DropdownMenuContent — no loading / empty state | dropdown-menu.tsx:32-50 | P1 | Content is a dumb pass-through with no loading or empty affordance. The data-table column-toggle menu (data-table.tsx:189-201) maps over columns with no guard; a menu driven by async-fetched items (a likely future consumer) would render an empty bordered box with no 'Loading…' or 'No options' message. M3 menus should communicate empty/loading rather than show a blank surface. | Provide a `DropdownMenuEmpty` helper and document a `loading` pattern (skeleton rows or a centered spinner inside Content). Consider a `DropdownMenuContent` `loading?`/`empty?` convenience that swaps children for a standardized state with proper `role="status"` / `aria-live` on the loading message. |
| DropdownMenuLabel — uppercase text without accessible casing | dropdown-menu.tsx:156 (`uppercase`) | P2 | Label forces CSS `uppercase`. Screen readers may read uppercased acronym-like words letter-by-letter, and the underlying text loses its natural casing only visually — acceptable, but combined with `text-xs` (12px) it also dips under comfortable legibility for a section header. data-table.tsx:190 relies on it for 'Toggle columns'. | Keep visual uppercase via CSS (preserves real text for AT, which is correct) but raise to `text-[0.6875rem]`/`text-xs` with `font-medium` already present and ensure adequate `tracking`. Lower priority since CSS uppercase does preserve DOM casing; flagging mainly for the small type size on a structural header. |
| DropdownMenu Root — no controlled-close helper / icon-only trigger a11y reminder | dropdown-menu.tsx:7-30 (Root/Trigger) + consumers nodes.tsx:237, data-table.tsx:183 | P2 | Both consumers use `DropdownMenuTrigger asChild` wrapping an icon-only button. The primitive provides no guard or convention ensuring those triggers carry an accessible name (`aria-label`/sr-only). Since this is the canonical kebab-menu trigger pattern, an unnamed icon button is a latent screen-reader gap that the primitive could help prevent. | Document the icon-trigger requirement in the primitive's usage notes and/or ship a `DropdownMenuIconTrigger` convenience that requires an `aria-label`. Verify nodes.tsx (line ~238 trigger button) and data-table.tsx column-toggle trigger expose a label; add sr-only text if missing. |

### components/ui/location-combobox.tsx

- verdict: **major** · 控件数: 8 · P0/P1/P2: 1/5/2
- topPriority: 控件无法关联外部 Label（缺 id/aria-labelledby）、触控目标低于 48dp、且缺 clearable/loading/disabled/size/i18n 等基础复用 prop —— 作为被表单复用的原语，这些缺陷会随每个调用方放大。

| 控件 | 位置 | 严重度 | 反模式 | 重设计方案 |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| 外部 Label 无法关联触发器（无障碍断链） | location-combobox.tsx:35-46 + 调用方 detail.tsx:245 | P0 | 调用方用 <Label>{t('location')}</Label> 但触发器是 role=combobox 的 Button，既无 id 也不接受 aria-labelledby/aria-label。Label 没有 htmlFor，点击 Label 不聚焦控件，屏幕阅读器朗读时只报 'combobox 折叠'，读不出字段名 '地区'。所有调用方都复刻这个断链。 | 新增 id?: string 与 ariaLabelledby?: string（或 'aria-label'）prop。把 id 透传到触发 Button，调用方 Label 用 htmlFor 指向它；或让控件内部用 aria-labelledby 关联外部 label id。补充 aria-haspopup="listbox"。 |
| 触控目标小于 M3 48dp 最小尺寸 | location-combobox.tsx:35-46（触发器）与 :59-67（选项行，继承 command.tsx CommandItem py-2.5≈42px） | P1 | 触发 Button 用默认 size（h-10=40px），下拉项 CommandItem 默认 py-2.5 约 42px，二者都低于 M3 触控目标 48dp。移动端点击精度差，列表项密集时误触。控件未暴露 size 调节，也没为移动端放大。 | 新增 size?: 'sm' \| 'default'，default 下触发器 min-h-12（48px），把 size 透传给 Button；下拉项加 min-h-12 类覆盖 CommandItem 默认 padding，保证行高≥48dp。 |
| 约 250 个选项全量渲染、无虚拟化无防抖 | location-combobox.tsx:57-77（options.map 一次性渲染全部） | P1 | LOCATION_OPTIONS 是完整 ISO-3166 国家表（约 250 项），options.map 一次性渲染所有 CommandItem 进 DOM。cmdk 每次按键对全量重算 filter 且无防抖，打开/输入有可感卡顿；列表 max-h 滚动但 DOM 节点不裁剪。作为通用控件，更大 options 会更糟。 | 对大列表启用虚拟化（cmdk + 虚拟滚动，或限制渲染前 N 项+'继续输入以缩小范围'提示）；CommandInput onValueChange 加 ~150ms 防抖；或新增 maxRendered?: number 上限。 |
| 缺 clearable 显式清除入口 | location-combobox.tsx:63-64（onSelect 里 opt.value===value?'':opt.value 的隐式 toggle） | P1 | 唯一清空方式是再次点中已选项触发 toggle 清空，这是隐藏交互——用户看不出'再点一次=清空'，发现性为零。M3 输入类控件应提供可见的清除（trailing X）。当前还得靠 options 里塞一个 value='' 的'（不设置）'伪选项来代偿清空，把数据污染进了选项表。 | 新增 clearable?: boolean，选中态时在 ChevronsUpDown 左侧显示可点击 X（带 aria-label='清除'，独立可聚焦，≥24px 命中区），点击 onChange('')。去掉隐式 toggle-clear，避免误清空；'（不设置）'不应作为业务选项混入。 |
| 缺 loading 与 disabled prop（异步与只读场景无解） | location-combobox.tsx:20-25（Props 仅 options/value/onChange/placeholder） | P1 | options 若来自异步加载，控件没有 loading 态：打开只会立刻显示 CommandEmpty '无匹配结果'，把'加载中'误报成'无结果'。也没有 disabled prop，无法在表单提交中/无权限时禁用触发器与清除。复用面越广这两个缺口越致命。 | 新增 loading?: boolean（true 时列表区显示带 spinner 的加载占位，抑制 CommandEmpty）与 disabled?: boolean（透传 Button disabled，关闭 Popover 触发）。区分三态：加载中 / 空数据源（options 为空）/ 有数据但无匹配。 |
| 内部文案硬编码中文、不可 i18n（违背可复用原语定位） | location-combobox.tsx:43 '选择...'、:54 '搜索...'、:56 '无匹配结果' | P1 | 占位回退、搜索框 placeholder、空态文案全是写死的中文字面量。项目本身有 i18n（调用方用 t()），但这个共享控件绕过翻译层，多语言下永远显示中文，且每个调用方无法定制。 | 新增 searchPlaceholder?: string 与 emptyText?: string prop（占位已有 placeholder），由调用方传 t() 值；控件不内置任何业务语言字面量，仅保留无文案的中性回退或要求必传。 |
| aria-controls 指向 Popover 容器而非真正的 listbox | location-combobox.tsx:39 aria-controls={listId} 指向 PopoverContent(:49)，而真实列表是 CommandList(:55) | P2 | aria-controls 指向 PopoverContent 外层容器，但承担 listbox 语义/选项 的是内部 CommandList。辅助技术按 aria-controls 跳转会落到容器而非选项列表；且未设置 aria-activedescendant 跟随高亮项，键盘用户的当前项不会被朗读。 | 把 listId 下放到 CommandList（其 role 应为 listbox），aria-controls 指向它；依赖 cmdk 暴露的 activedescendant 或显式接线 aria-activedescendant，使键盘上下移动时朗读当前候选。 |
| 空数据源与无匹配未区分；无 name 表单集成 | location-combobox.tsx:56（CommandEmpty）与 Props(:20-25) | P2 | options=[] 时与'搜索无匹配'共用同一句'无匹配结果'，语义错位（数据没来 vs 搜不到）。控件也不接受 name，无法在原生/受控表单中作为命名字段提交，复用到表单库时需额外包装。 | 区分 options.length===0 的空数据态文案与搜索无匹配文案；新增 name?: string（渲染隐藏 input 承载 value）或 required?: boolean 以便表单校验与提交。 |

### components/ui/checkbox.tsx

- verdict: **major** · 控件数: 4 · P0/P1/P2: 2/1/1
- topPriority: 触控目标只有 18dp,远低于 M3 的 48dp 最小值,且没有不可见命中区扩展——影响 data-table 行选择和 gateway 多选弹层等所有调用方,移动端极难点中。

| 控件 | 位置 | 严重度 | 反模式 | 重设计方案 |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Checkbox 触控目标尺寸 | components/ui/checkbox.tsx:14-15 (size-[18px]) | P0 | 复选框可点区域被硬定为 size-[18px](18dp),没有任何不可见命中区(::before/伪元素)扩展。M3 规范要求所有交互控件触控目标 ≥48dp。data-table 的行/全选列与 gateway 弹层里 Checkbox 直接裸用,移动端 18dp 的命中区几乎不可能精准点中,且相邻行复选框间距过小易误触。视觉上保持 18dp 没问题,但命中区必须独立放大。 | 视觉方块保持 18dp 不变,新增一个不可见的 48x48 命中层:在 Root 上加 before 伪元素 'before:absolute before:left-1/2 before:top-1/2 before:size-12 before:-translate-x-1/2 before:-translate-y-1/2 before:content-[""]',并把 Root 设为 relative(已是 relative)。或暴露 size 变体('sm'=20dp 视觉/'md'=24dp)同时命中区恒为 48dp。确保命中层不影响 flex 布局(伪元素 absolute 不占位)。 |
| indeterminate(半选)状态语义 | components/ui/checkbox.tsx:25-30; 调用方 data-table.tsx:108-112 | P0 | Indicator 内永远渲染 CheckIcon,完全没处理 Radix 原生支持的 checked="indeterminate"。data-table 的全选表头用的是 getIsAllPageRowsSelected()(布尔),当本页只选中部分行时,标准 M3/桌面交互应显示横线(–)的半选态,这里无法表达——用户看到全选框是「未勾」,但实际已选若干行,反馈与真实状态不符,且 ARIA 也不会播报 mixed。 | 在 Indicator 内按状态切换图标:data-[state=indeterminate] 显示 MinusIcon,data-[state=checked] 显示 CheckIcon(可用两个带 data-state 条件 class 的 Indicator,或读 props.checked 决定)。同步把 data-table 全选 checked 改为 'all \| indeterminate(部分) \| false',onCheckedChange 配合 toggleAllPageRowsSelected。Radix 会自动把 aria-checked 设为 'mixed',无障碍随之正确。 |
| 标签关联与可达性 API | components/ui/checkbox.tsx:7-33 (组件签名) | P1 | 组件只透传 props,不提供任何标签关联帮助。两个调用方各自手写:data-table 靠 aria-label(可接受),gateway 靠外层 <label> 包裹(可接受),但原语本身没有约束,后续调用方很容易既不传 aria-label 也不关联 label,产出无可访问名的复选框。对一个被多页面复用的控件,缺少「无可访问名时的兜底/告警」是隐患。 | 提供可选的 label/id 便捷 API:接受 label?: ReactNode,内部渲染 <span id> 并自动 aria-labelledby 关联;或至少在开发态对「既无 aria-label 又无 aria-labelledby 且无关联 label」做 console.warn。保留纯受控用法的同时降低调用方踩坑概率。 |
| 缺失 size / loading / 描述性 props | components/ui/checkbox.tsx:7-10 | P2 | 作为共享原语,没有 size 变体(全站只有一种 18dp,密集表格与表单同尺寸,无法适配触控密度)、没有 loading 态(异步切换如行级开关在请求期间无法表达 pending,也不能临时禁用防重复点击)。导致调用方要么手改 className 破坏一致性,要么自行在外层套 spinner。 | 加 size?: 'sm'\|'md'(视觉 18/24,命中区恒 48);加 loading?: boolean,为 true 时 Indicator 区域渲染小 spinner 并禁用交互(disabled 语义 + aria-busy),避免异步选择被连点。这些是可选 prop,默认行为不变,向后兼容。 |

### components/ui/input.tsx

- verdict: **major** · 控件数: 6 · P0/P1/P2: 1/3/2
- topPriority: Hard-coded h-10 (40px) is below the M3 48dp touch target and is the only height the primitive offers; since every form field and the data-table search box renders through this component, all 17 callers ship a sub-spec mobile tap target with no way to opt into a comfortable size. Fix by introducing a size prop with a default that meets 48dp on touch.

| 控件 | 位置 | 严重度 | 反模式 | 重设计方案 |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Input root — fixed height | components/ui/input.tsx:11 ("h-10 ...") | P0 | Height is locked to h-10 (40px) with no size prop. M3 spec and the review brief require touch targets >= 48dp. Every caller (login, portal forms, users/customers/plans dialogs, and the data-table search field at data-table.tsx:169) inherits a 40px hit area, so the violation is fleet-wide and unfixable from call sites without className hacks. | Add a size variant via cva: size='md' (default, h-12 / 48px to satisfy M3 touch), size='sm' (h-10, opt-in for dense desktop tables only). Keep text-base on mobile (prevents iOS zoom), md:text-sm on >=md. Density-sensitive callers like data-table can pass size='sm' explicitly; default path is spec-compliant. |
| Input — no adornment / icon slots, no clearable | components/ui/input.tsx:5-19; consumed by data-table.tsx:166-175 | P1 | The primitive accepts only native input props, so data-table hand-rolls a leading Search icon with absolute positioning + pl-10 and offers no clear button. Every search/filter consumer must re-implement icon alignment, and there is no 'X to clear' affordance, forcing users to select-all-delete to reset a filter. | Wrap input in a relative container and add startIcon?/endIcon? slots plus clearable?: boolean. When clearable && value, render a focusable clear button (>=48dp hit area, aria-label='Clear', type='button') that fires onChange with empty value and refocuses the field. data-table search collapses to <Input startIcon={<Search/>} clearable value={...} />. |
| Input — validation: no error/helper text slot or aria-describedby wiring | components/ui/input.tsx:13 (aria-invalid styling only) | P1 | The primitive styles aria-invalid but provides no mechanism to attach an error or helper message, and no auto-generated id. Callers must manually pair <Label htmlFor> (e.g. users.tsx:432, portal/login.tsx:132) and there is no association between the field and any error string, so screen-reader users get a red ring with no announced reason. WCAG 3.3.1/4.1.3 gap across all forms. | Add optional error?: string and helperText?: string props. Auto-generate an id (React.useId) if none passed; render helper/error in a <p> with that id and wire aria-describedby + aria-invalid automatically. Error text uses text-md-error; assertive live region so it is announced on change. Label association can be encouraged via a thin labeled Field wrapper but at minimum the describedby plumbing must be built in. |
| Search-type Input — no debounce | components/ui/data-table.tsx:169-174 (onChange -> onSearchChange every keystroke) | P1 | Because the primitive is a raw controlled input, the data-table fires onSearchChange on every keystroke and filters live. On larger lists this thrashes render/filtering per character and there is no built-in debounce the primitive could provide for search semantics. | Add a debounceMs?: number prop on Input (or a thin SearchInput composed from it). When set, keep an internal value for instant typing and debounce the onChange/onValueChange callback (default ~250ms). data-table opts in with debounceMs={250}, decoupling typing responsiveness from filter cost. |
| Password Input — no reveal toggle | pages/login.tsx, pages/portal/login.tsx:153, register/reset-password (type="password" via this primitive) | P2 | Password fields render through the same bare Input with no show/hide affordance anywhere in the app (grep for showPassword/Eye returns nothing). Users cannot verify what they typed, raising auth friction and error rates on touch keyboards. | When type='password', auto-render a trailing reveal toggle (Eye/EyeOff, type='button', aria-pressed, aria-label 'Show/Hide password', >=48dp) that swaps type between password/text. Reuse the endIcon slot so it composes with the clearable work rather than each login page hand-rolling it. |
| Input — no loading / busy state | components/ui/input.tsx (no loading prop) | P2 | Async-validated or async-suggest fields (e.g. uniqueness checks, location lookups) have no standard busy affordance; callers would have to overlay their own spinner, leading to inconsistent or missing feedback during in-flight validation. | Add loading?: boolean that renders a trailing spinner in the endIcon position and sets aria-busy='true'. Keep input editable during load unless caller also disables. Pairs with the adornment slot so no extra layout work for consumers. |

### components/ui/textarea.tsx

- verdict: **major** · 控件数: 6 · P0/P1/P2: 0/3/3
- topPriority: Add first-class supporting/error text + character counter wired through aria-describedby. Right now the primitive paints an aria-invalid red border with zero programmatically-associated message, and every long free-text field (ticket body, ticket reply, announcement content) has no length feedback. This is the single change that fixes both the worst a11y gap and the worst UX gap across all 4 callers at once.

| 控件 | 位置 | 严重度 | 反模式 | 重设计方案 |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Textarea — error/supporting text association | components/ui/textarea.tsx:5-16 (consumed at pages/portal/tickets/[id].tsx:183-188, pages/portal/tickets.tsx:305-311, announcements.tsx) | P1 | Primitive exposes aria-invalid styling (red border + ring) but no message slot. Every caller renders its error as a sibling <p>/<div> (e.g. sendError, submitError) that is NOT linked to the field via aria-describedby, and the textarea never receives aria-invalid when those errors fire. A screen-reader user gets a silent red box; the validation text is an orphaned node elsewhere in the DOM. | Add `helperText`, `errorText`, and `invalid` props. Render a supporting-text region below the field; auto-generate an id and set aria-describedby on the textarea; set aria-invalid={invalid \|\| !!errorText}. Error text replaces helper text and uses md-error color + role for live announcement. Callers stop hand-rolling error <p> nodes. |
| Textarea — character counter / maxLength | components/ui/textarea.tsx:5-16 (ticket reply [id].tsx:173, ticket create tickets.tsx:296, announcement content announcements.tsx:374) | P1 | No maxLength support and no character counter. All three free-text bodies are unbounded in the UI; if the backend enforces a length the user only discovers it on a failed submit. M3 text fields treat the character counter (e.g. 120/500) as a first-class supporting-text affordance, which is entirely absent. | Expose `maxLength` and a `showCount` prop. When set, render a right-aligned counter in the supporting-text row (current/max), turn it md-error when within the last threshold or over limit, and set the native maxLength on the textarea. Counter shares the aria-describedby region so it is announced. |
| Textarea — submit-on-modifier-Enter affordance | pages/portal/tickets/[id].tsx:179-181 vs pages/tickets/[id].tsx:227 vs pages/portal/tickets.tsx:296 / announcements.tsx:374 | P1 | Ctrl/Cmd+Enter-to-send is reimplemented inline in the portal reply box (onKeyDown at [id].tsx:179) but missing from the other reply/create surfaces, so the keyboard submit shortcut is inconsistent across identical-looking textareas. Even where present there is no visible hint, so the shortcut is undiscoverable. | Add an optional `onSubmit` prop; when provided, the primitive handles ⌘/Ctrl+Enter centrally and (optionally via `submitHint`) renders a muted 'Press ⌘+Enter to send' hint in the supporting-text row. Removes per-page divergence and makes the shortcut discoverable. |
| Textarea — auto-resize vs fixed rows conflict | components/ui/textarea.tsx:10 (field-sizing-content + min-h-20) overridden by every caller with resize-none + rows | P2 | The base class enables `field-sizing-content` (content auto-grow), but all four callers override it with `resize-none` plus a fixed `rows` value, so the auto-grow behavior never actually runs and the user also loses the manual resize handle. The control ships two contradictory sizing models and no caller gets a coherent one. | Pick one model in the primitive: keep field-sizing-content as default auto-grow with a built-in `max-h` cap so long content scrolls instead of pushing the page, and expose an explicit `resizable` (default true → resize-y) prop. Drop the need for callers to pass resize-none/rows; offer `minRows`/`maxRows` instead for predictable growth bounds. |
| Textarea — required / accessible-name guard | components/ui/textarea.tsx:5-16 (Label rendered as detached sibling at tickets.tsx:295, announcements.tsx:373) | P2 | Primitive has no built-in id or label wiring; callers place a <Label> as a plain sibling with no htmlFor/id pairing, so clicking the label does not focus the field and the field may have no programmatic accessible name. Required fields also have no aria-required path. | Accept/auto-generate `id`, expose `required` (sets aria-required and an optional visual marker), and document the Label htmlFor pairing. Optionally provide a thin labelled wrapper so callers cannot forget the association. |
| Textarea — busy/submitting state | components/ui/textarea.tsx (callers gate only the submit button: tickets/[id].tsx:192 disabled={sending...}) | P2 | No `loading`/`busy` affordance. During async submit the field stays fully editable while only the button is disabled, so a user can keep typing or fire the inline ⌘+Enter handler mid-request, risking a double-submit. No aria-busy is exposed. | Add a `busy`/`readOnly`-driven state that the primitive can reflect with aria-busy and (optionally) a non-interactive overlay, and have the ⌘+Enter handler no-op while busy, so submit state is coordinated at the control rather than only on the button. |

### components/layout/Sidebar.tsx

- verdict: **major** · 控件数: 9 · P0/P1/P2: 1/3/5
- topPriority: No responsive behavior whatsoever: Sidebar is hard-rendered as a fixed w-60 shrink-0 column in AppLayout with zero breakpoints, no hamburger/drawer, and no collapse. On phones/tablets it permanently steals 240px and cannot be dismissed, making every admin page fail the mobile-reachability bar. This is the one fix that unblocks all touch usage.

| 控件 | 位置 | 严重度 | 反模式 | 重设计方案 |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Sidebar container (whole aside) — responsive strategy | Sidebar.tsx:68 (aside w-60 shrink-0) + AppLayout.tsx:42 (renders <Sidebar/> unconditionally) | P0 | aside is 'flex h-screen w-60 shrink-0' with no breakpoint prefixes; AppLayout places it as a permanent flex column. There is no hamburger trigger, no off-canvas drawer, no overlay, no md:/lg: hiding anywhere in the repo. On <768px the nav eats 240px of a ~360px viewport and content is crushed; there is no way to hide or reach a collapsed nav. | Make Sidebar a controlled responsive primitive: render as a static rail at lg+ (lg:flex) and as a Radix Dialog/Sheet drawer below lg (hidden lg:flex on the static one + a portal'd overlay drawer). Add a header hamburger IconButton in AppLayout (aria-label, aria-expanded, aria-controls) that opens the drawer; trap focus, close on route change and Esc, restore focus to trigger. Lift open state into AppLayout or a NavContext. |
| Nav item (renderNavItem) — touch target height | Sidebar.tsx:54 (px-4 py-2.5 ... text-sm) | P1 | py-2.5 (10px) + 20px line-height ≈ 40px row height, below the M3 48dp minimum. On touch the rows are cramped and mis-tap-prone, and this is the most-used control in the app. | Guarantee ≥48dp: min-h-12 (48px) with py-3, keep the pill radius. Optionally expose a size prop ('default'\|'compact') so dense desktop users can opt into 40px while touch defaults to 48px via a media-query token. Verify the 48px also applies inside the mobile drawer. |
| Locale segmented toggle buttons | Sidebar.tsx:94-108 (px-3 py-1.5 text-xs buttons in a flex group) | P1 | Buttons are ~28px tall (py-1.5 text-xs) — far under 48dp, the smallest touch targets in the chrome. They also sit in a bare <div> with no group semantics, so screen readers announce two unrelated pressed buttons with no relationship and no group name. | Raise each segment to min-h-12 (or min-h-11) on touch. Wrap the pair in role="group" (or role="radiogroup" with role="radio"+aria-checked) and give it an accessible name (aria-label localized 'Language'/'语言'). Segmented-button single-select semantics read more correctly as radio than two aria-pressed toggles. |
| Permission-gated nav list — loading/empty state | Sidebar.tsx:12,38-39 (useCurrentUser) + 87 (animate-slide-up) | P1 | While useCurrentUser is resolving, user is undefined so perm-gated items are filtered out; the sidebar first paints only the perm:null base items, then pops the rest in (with the slide-up animation re-firing) once the user loads. This is a visible content-shift/flash on every cold load and there is no skeleton or pending affordance. | Add an explicit loading branch: when user is undefined render fixed-height skeleton rows (matching final 48px height/count) instead of a partial list, so the nav does not reflow. Only run the staggered animation after data is ready. Expose a loading prop on the primitive so the drawer variant behaves identically. |
| nav landmark accessible name | Sidebar.tsx:77 (aria-label="主导航") | P2 | The nav landmark label is hardcoded Chinese, so English-locale screen-reader users hear '主导航'. The app is fully i18n'd (next-intl) everywhere else, so this is an inconsistent untranslated string in an a11y-critical spot. | Use tNav('mainNavigation') (add the key for zh/en). Same for the mobile drawer dialog title and the hamburger aria-label. |
| Truncated nav labels — no overflow affordance | Sidebar.tsx:62 (span truncate) | P2 | Labels use truncate inside a 240px rail. Long localized strings (German-length or future labels) get clipped with an ellipsis and no way to read the full text — no title attr, no tooltip, and nothing for keyboard/SR users. | Add title={label} on the link (cheap) or wrap in components/ui/tooltip showing the full label on hover/focus. In a future collapsed/icon-rail mode the tooltip becomes mandatory, so build it into the NavItem primitive now. |
| Brand / logo header | Sidebar.tsx:69-76 (div with Globe + title, not interactive) | P2 | The product brand block is a static div. Users conventionally expect the top-left logo to navigate to dashboard/home; here it is dead, and there is also no skip-to-content link before the long nav for keyboard users. | Wrap the brand in a Link to /dashboard (with focus-visible ring and an aria-label). Consider adding a visually-hidden 'skip to main content' link at the top of AppLayout that targets the <main>. |
| Active-route detection | Sidebar.tsx:45-46 (pathname === href \|\| startsWith(href + '/')) | P2 | Prefix matching on router.pathname is brittle: sibling routes that share a prefix (e.g. a future /nodes vs /nodes-archive, or query-only states) can both light up or none light up for dynamic segments. It also won't reflect the active item inside the mobile drawer if state isn't shared. | Match on path segments (split and compare the first segment) rather than raw startsWith, and ensure the same isActive logic feeds both rail and drawer NavItems via the shared primitive. |
| Admin section label fallback | Sidebar.tsx:84 (tNav('admin') \|\| 'Admin') | P2 | next-intl t() never returns a falsy value (it returns the key or throws on missing), so the '\|\| Admin' fallback is dead code that masks a missing-key error and misleads future maintainers into thinking fallbacks work this way. | Drop the \|\| 'Admin' and rely on the translation key existing (add it to the message catalogs). If a runtime-safe fallback is wanted, use t.has('admin') or the i18n getMessageFallback config, not a JS \|\|. |

### components/portal/PortalLayout.tsx

- verdict: **major** · 控件数: 8 · P0/P1/P2: 0/5/3
- topPriority: Replace the hand-rolled user dropdown (lines 89-129) with the existing Radix DropdownMenu primitive. The custom implementation loses every a11y affordance Radix gives for free (focus trap, focus return, Escape-to-close, arrow-key roving, role=menu, aria-haspopup/expanded) and introduces a phantom full-screen tab stop via the invisible backdrop button. Since this shell wraps every portal page, the defect is repeated on every screen.

| 控件 | 位置 | 严重度 | 反模式 | 重设计方案 |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| User account dropdown (desktop) | lines 89-129 | P1 | Hand-rolled disclosure: useState(userMenuOpen) + an absolutely-positioned panel + a `fixed inset-0` invisible <button aria-label> as the outside-click catcher. No focus trap, no focus return to trigger on close, no Escape handling, no arrow-key navigation, trigger lacks aria-haspopup/aria-expanded, panel lacks role=menu / menuitem roles. The full-screen backdrop button is itself focusable, inserting a meaningless tab stop over the whole viewport. | Delete the entire custom block and compose components/ui/dropdown-menu.tsx: <DropdownMenu><DropdownMenuTrigger asChild><button ...avatar/></DropdownMenuTrigger><DropdownMenuContent align="end"><DropdownMenuLabel>{name/email}</DropdownMenuLabel><DropdownMenuSeparator/><DropdownMenuItem asChild><Link href="/portal/account">…</Link></DropdownMenuItem><DropdownMenuItem variant="destructive" onSelect={...}>logout</DropdownMenuItem></DropdownMenuContent></DropdownMenu>. Drop userMenuOpen state entirely; Radix manages open/close, outside-click, Escape, focus. |
| Logout action (desktop + mobile) | lines 118-124, 182-188, handleLogout 11-14 | P1 | Session-ending destructive action fires on a single click with zero confirmation and zero feedback. handleLogout is async (awaits portalLogout) but the button never enters a disabled/loading state, so a double-click fires two logout requests, and the user sees no progress before the hard window.location redirect. No try/catch — a failed logout silently strips the UI affordance with no error toast. | Add a confirm step (AlertDialog/confirm dialog) OR at minimum guard with an isLoggingOut state: disable the menu item, show an inline spinner, wrap portalLogout in try/catch and surface failures via toast. Use the dropdown/button `loading`+`disabled` pattern so the control is idempotent against double-click. |
| Language segmented toggle (desktop 71-86 + mobile 163-178) | lines 71-86, 163-178 | P1 | Two plain <button> groups acting as a single-select control with no semantic grouping: no role="radiogroup"/role="radio", no aria-pressed/aria-checked, no aria-label on the group or buttons. A screen-reader user cannot tell which locale is active or that the two buttons are mutually exclusive. Active state is conveyed by background color only. Buttons are px-3 py-1 (~24px tall) — far below the 48dp M3 touch target, and the mobile copy is the worst offender since it is touch-only. Logic is duplicated verbatim in two places. | Extract a <LocaleToggle> control. Wrap in a container with role="radiogroup" aria-label={t('language')}, give each button role="radio" aria-checked={locale===l} and an aria-label, and add aria-pressed. Bump tap area to min-h-12 (or min-w/min-h 48px) on the mobile instance via a size prop. Single source of truth reused by both desktop and mobile. |
| Primary navigation links (desktop + mobile) | lines 49-65, 146-162 | P1 | Active route is computed via isActive() but exposed only as a color swap — no aria-current="page". Screen-reader/keyboard users get no indication of current location. Desktop links are py-2 (~32px) and the row is dense; the active styling is the only differentiator. | Add aria-current={isActive(href) ? 'page' : undefined} to each Link in both the desktop and mobile nav maps. Ensure mobile nav rows meet min-h-12 (they are py-3 ≈ 44px — nudge to 48dp). |
| Mobile menu disclosure + hamburger | lines 131-138, 143-193 | P1 | Hamburger button has aria-label="Toggle menu" but no aria-expanded={mobileOpen} and no aria-controls pointing at the panel, and the label is hardcoded English (not via t()). The expanded panel has no focus management: opening it does not move focus inside, Escape does not close it, background scroll is not locked, and tapping outside the panel does not dismiss it (only the X or selecting a nav item closes it). Hamburger is h-10 w-10 (40px) < 48dp. | Add aria-expanded={mobileOpen} aria-controls="portal-mobile-nav" to the hamburger and localize its label via t(). Give the panel id="portal-mobile-nav". Either adopt a Radix-backed disclosure/Sheet so focus trap + Escape + scroll-lock come for free, or add a keydown(Escape) handler, focus-move-on-open, body scroll lock, and an outside-click dismissal. Bump hamburger to h-12 w-12. |
| Outside-click backdrop (user menu) | line 103 | P2 | `<button aria-label="关闭菜单">` — hardcoded Chinese string in an otherwise i18n-driven component, and it is a focusable full-viewport element that becomes a tab stop. Inconsistent with the localized t() usage everywhere else. | Removed entirely when migrating to Radix DropdownMenu (Radix handles dismissal without a focusable overlay). If kept anywhere, source the label from t() and mark aria-hidden / tabIndex=-1. |
| Customer auth loading / empty state | lines 89, 179 (customer && …) | P2 | The user dropdown and mobile logout are gated on `customer &&`, so during the auth fetch the navbar renders with no user affordance and silently pops it in once loaded — no skeleton, no reserved space, causing layout shift and a moment where the user appears logged-out. | Render a skeleton avatar/placeholder while the customer query is loading (reserve the slot), and only fall back to the empty render for the genuinely-unauthenticated case. Expose loading from useCustomer(). |
| Page-level keyboard navigation (skip link) | lines 36-37, 196 | P2 | <main> exists as a landmark but there is no skip-to-content link, so keyboard users must tab through the full brand + 6 nav items + lang toggle + user menu on every single portal page before reaching content. | Add a visually-hidden-until-focused skip link as the first focusable element (`<a href="#portal-main" class="sr-only focus:not-sr-only …">`) and give <main> id="portal-main" tabIndex={-1}. |

## 3. 页面改动

### 3.1 管理端 (admin)

#### pages/dashboard.tsx

- verdict: **major** · 控件数: 13 · P0/P1/P2: 1/4/8
- topPriority: P0: 数据加载无 error/catch 分支(dashboard.tsx:90-94),API 失败时静默吞错,页面显示全 0 数据(0 nodes / 0 online / 0 offline),管理员会把「后端挂了」误判为「机群正常无节点」——这是会导致根本性运维误判的 silent failure,必须最先修。

| 控件 | 位置 | 严重度 | 反模式 | 重设计方案 |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Dashboard 数据加载缺 error state(silent failure) | pages/dashboard.tsx:90-94 | P0 | sessionApi(AdminService.nodesList({})).then(setNodes).finally(setLoading(false)) 无 .catch。API 失败时 nodes 保持 [],loading=false,页面渲染 0 total / 0 online / 0 offline + 空表,与「真实空机群」视觉完全一致。管理员无法区分『后端宕机』与『确实没有节点』,造成根本性运维误判。三份审查一致标为最高优先级。 | 加 const [error, setError] = useState<unknown>(null);在 useEffect 内 .catch((e) => setError(e))。渲染顺序:loading → skeleton;!loading && error → 错误态(AlertTriangle 图标 + 文案『无法加载机群数据』+ <Button onClick={refetch}>重试</Button>,把 fetch 抽成可复用的 loadNodes 函数供重试调用);!loading && !error → 正常内容。错误文案走 i18n。 |
| Recently Registered 表格行 — 虚假可点 affordance + 无钻取路径 | pages/dashboard.tsx:243-265 | P1 | TableRow 带 hover-state(hover 背景变化)暗示可点,但无 onClick / 无 Link 包裹 / 无 cursor-pointer / 无 tabIndex。用户看到节点实体行,最自然操作是点行看详情,点下去却无反应(违反 Nielsen #1)。键盘与 SR 用户完全无路径进入节点详情。三份审查全部点名。 | 给每个 TableRow 加导航能力:onClick={() => router.push(`/nodes/${n.mac}`)} + cursor-pointer + tabIndex={0} + onKeyDown 处理 Enter/Space。同时为整表加 aria-label="最近注册的节点",并加 role/语义让 SR 知道行可激活。若节点详情路由暂不存在,则改为在 Card footer 加『查看全部节点』Link 指向 /nodes,绝不保留无任何出口的静态实体行。 |
| Online Rate 进度条 — 缺 role="progressbar" + 无精确基数 + 无阈值警示 | pages/dashboard.tsx:192-200 | P1 | 纯 <div class="h-2"> 嵌套填充 div,无 role="progressbar" / aria-valuenow / aria-valuemin / aria-valuemax / aria-label。SR 直接跳过这个关键健康指标(违反 WCAG 4.1.2)。且只显示百分比不显示基数(12/15),低健康度时也无色彩升级,色盲/SR 用户无法感知严重性。 | 外层加 role="progressbar" aria-valuenow={onlineCount} aria-valuemin={0} aria-valuemax={nodes.length} aria-label={`${pct}% 节点在线`};内层填充 div 加 aria-hidden="true"。百分比旁补精确数字『{onlineCount}/{nodes.length}』。阈值色彩:onlineRate<60% 填充用 bg-md-error 并加 text-md-error 文案;60-80% 维持当前 tertiary;>80% 维持。注:阈值色彩属信息编码而非纯配色,不与已定稿视觉冲突。 |
| TopBar Logout — destructive 操作无二次确认 | components/layout/AppLayout.tsx:28-34,47-55 | P1 | Logout 按钮 onClick 直接 handleLogout(),无 confirm。ghost variant 与旁边 ThemeToggle 视觉权重相同,误触即登出并丢失 SPA 状态(window.location.href 硬跳转)。M3 destructive flow 规范要求确认或可撤销。 | 二选一:(a) 加 Dialog 二次确认——const [showLogout,setShowLogout]=useState(false),按钮改 onClick={()=>setShowLogout(true)},Dialog 内『确认退出登录?』+ Cancel / 确认(destructive variant)按钮;(b) 或保留直接登出但改为 M3 snackbar-with-action 的 undo toast(5s 内可撤销)。优先 (a),实现简单且语义明确。 |
| 页面加载态 — 全屏 spinner 而非骨架屏 | pages/dashboard.tsx:134-141 | P1 | loading 时整页只显示居中 circular spinner,数据到达后内容突然替换,产生 CLS 与内容跳变,违反 M3 perceived-performance / progressive disclosure。spinner 容器还缺 role="status" + aria-label,SR 无法感知『正在加载』。 | 替换为结构匹配的 skeleton:4 张 StatsCard 灰色占位(bg-md-surface-container-high + shimmer)+ Online Rate 条占位 + 5 行表格占位,布局与最终内容一致以消除 CLS。若保留 spinner 作为兜底,给其容器加 role="status" aria-label="正在加载节点数据"(role=status 隐含 aria-live=polite,加载完成消失时会被播报)。 |
| 4 张 StatsCard — 无钻取入口 | pages/dashboard.tsx:145-174,StatsCard 29-46 | P2 | 四张统计卡纯展示,无 onClick / 无键盘可达。Dashboard 最高频需求是『看数字→点进去看明细』,Online/Offline 是巡检第一入口,当前断了第一跳。三份审查一致认为是 minor 增强,且依赖下游筛选路由是否存在。 | 若 /nodes 支持 query 筛选,则把 Online/Offline/New 卡改为 Link 或 <button> 包裹整卡:Total→/nodes,Online→/nodes?status=online,Offline→/nodes?status=offline,New→/nodes?within=7d。整卡作为触控目标(已 py-5,达 48dp),加 aria-label(如『查看 5 个在线节点』)+ hover state-layer/轻微 elevation 提示可点。若筛选路由未实现则暂保持展示态,不加假 affordance。 |
| 入场动画无视 prefers-reduced-motion | pages/dashboard.tsx:33,125,138,179,207,246 + 全局 animate-* 类 | P2 | animate-slide-up / animate-fade-in / animate-spin 及 animationDelay 硬编码,经核查 styles/globals.css 不含任何 @media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce) 守卫。前庭障碍用户无法关闭动效,违反 WCAG 2.3.3 / M3 motion 规范。影响全站非仅本页。 | 在 styles/globals.css 末尾加全局守卫:@media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce) { *, *::before, *::after { animation-duration: 0.01ms !important; animation-iteration-count: 1 !important; transition-duration: 0.01ms !important; } } 或针对 .animate-slide-up/.animate-fade-in/.animate-scale-in 设 animation:none,.animate-spin 设极短 duration。一处修全局生效。 |
| TopBar UserBadge — 像可点实则静态 | components/layout/AppLayout.tsx:11-22,45 | P2 | UserBadge 是 avatar + username 经典『点我下拉』模式,用户预期点击看到 profile/settings/logout,但当前是纯 <div>,无 onClick / role / tabIndex,SR 也无法识别。虚假 affordance(Nielsen #1)。 | 将 UserBadge 改为 <button> 触发 DropdownMenu,菜单含『我的资料』『设置』『退出登录』(把 header 的 Logout 收纳进此菜单,统一账户操作入口),退出仍走上面 P1 的二次确认。改后 header 右侧只剩 ThemeToggle + UserBadge 菜单,视觉更聚焦。 |
| 空态无 CTA + 未区分『无任何节点』与『本周无新增』 | pages/dashboard.tsx:216-220 | P2 | recentNodes.length===0 时只显示 Server 图标 + 一句『本周无新增节点』,无任何 CTA,用户卡死此页。且该空态在『整个机群为空(nodes.length===0)』与『有节点但本周无新增』两种语义下显示相同文案,缺乏针对性引导。容器也缺 role="status"。 | 区分两态:nodes.length===0 → 文案『还没有节点』+ <Button variant="outline" onClick={()=>router.push('/nodes')}>注册首个节点 / 查看节点</Button>;nodes.length>0 && recentNodes.length===0 → 维持『本周无新增』信息文案 + 『查看全部节点』Link。空态容器加 role="status" aria-label={空态文案},新增时被 polite 播报。 |
| 数据无刷新/陈旧(无 polling、无手动刷新、全量无分页) | pages/dashboard.tsx:90-94,147 | P2 | nodesList({}) 一次性全量拉取,无 polling/SWR 失效,Dashboard 数字是 snapshot 非 live,管理员看到的『5 在线』可能是 10 分钟前;无请求取消易拿 stale closure;节点上千时全量入内存且响应慢。 | 引入 SWR/React Query:useSWR('nodes', () => sessionApi(AdminService.nodesList({})), { refreshInterval: 30000 }),自带 retry/cache/error/loading(可同时覆盖上面 P0 error 态与 P1 loading 态)。副标题右侧加 <Button variant="ghost" onClick={()=>mutate()}>刷新</Button> + 『最近更新: {time}』提示数据新鲜度。recentNodes 理想由服务端算(?sort=-registered_at&limit=10&since=7d),前端仅展示。 |
| Status Badge — 缺 role="status" 与 Unknown 排查引导 | pages/dashboard.tsx:61-79,258 | P2 | Badge 颜色+文字双信号已合规,但包裹 span 无 role="status"/aria-label,SR 把『Online/Offline』当孤立词读,失去『这是节点状态』语境。Unknown 态无任何排查 hint,用户不知为何没上报、怎么查。 | 给 badge span 加 aria-label={`节点状态: ${probeStatus}`}(避免孤立词)。Unknown badge 旁加 Info 图标 + Tooltip『该节点超过 24h 未上报,请检查连通性』。注:Badge 若改用 components/ui/badge.tsx 共享原语承载这些语义,需在原语层支持透传 aria-label/role。 |
| Recently Registered 表格 — 缺 caption、无排序 | pages/dashboard.tsx:222-268 | P2 | Table 无 <TableCaption> 供 SR 说明用途;Registered At 看似默认排序但用户无法切换排序列。table.tsx 已支持 caption-bottom,缺的是使用。 | 在 <Table> 内加 <TableCaption>{t('recentlyRegistered')}</TableCaption>(可视觉隐藏)。排序为后续迭代:若启用,优先用现有 components/ui/data-table.tsx(已具排序能力)替换裸 Table,而非在裸 Table 上手搓;排序列头设 aria-sort=ascending\|descending\|none。本页 10 行小表排序为低优,caption 先补。 |
| Sidebar — 缺 skip-to-content + 焦点指示与 active fill 未区分 + 语言切换组缺 role=group | components/layout/Sidebar.tsx:48-65,77,92-110 + main 区 AppLayout.tsx:57 | P2 | 1) 无 skip link,键盘用户须 Tab 穿过整列导航才到 main(违反 WCAG 2.4.1)。2) nav item active 仅靠 bg-md-secondary-container 填充表达,focus-visible ring 与 active fill 视觉接近,键盘焦点在已激活项上辨识度低。3) 语言切换两按钮已正确用 aria-pressed,但外层 div 缺 role="group" aria-label,SR 无法感知『这是一组二选一』。 | 1) 在 Sidebar 顶部加 <a href="#main-content" class="sr-only focus:not-sr-only ...">跳到主内容</a>,并给 AppLayout 的 <main> 加 id="main-content" tabIndex={-1}。2) 确保 focus-visible:ring 在 active 项上仍清晰(可加 ring-offset 或在 active 态用不同 ring 色),让焦点独立于选中态可辨。3) 语言切换容器 div 加 role="group" aria-label="语言 / Language"。 |

#### pages/nodes.tsx

- verdict: **major** · 控件数: 18 · P0/P1/P2: 2/6/10
- topPriority: 用可访问的 Dialog 替换两处原生 window.confirm()（单行删除 + 批量删除），批量删除改为 Promise.allSettled 并列出受影响节点、回报成功/失败数量——这是唯一同时命中破坏性操作确认、无障碍焦点陷阱、静默吞错三项 P0 的改动。

| 控件 | 位置 | 严重度 | 反模式 | 重设计方案 |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| 单行 Delete 菜单项 | nodes.tsx:166 (handleDelete) + 250-254 (DropdownMenuItem) | P0 | 破坏性删除走原生 window.confirm()。该弹窗不 trap 焦点、无 aria-describedby 说明后果、dark mode 下样式失控、与 Radix 键盘行为不一致；确认仅靠 i18n 文案，无二次校验。 | 改为 role=alertdialog 的 Dialog：标题=删除节点，正文带 error 图标 + 明确列出 mac/hostname + 不可逆提示，焦点默认落在 Cancel，确认按钮用 destructive variant。删除成功/失败用 aria-live 内联反馈。 |
| 批量删除按钮 + batchAction('delete') | nodes.tsx:175-184 (batchAction) + 410-417 (Button) | P0 | 三连缺陷：(1) 原生 confirm() 仅显示数量、不列具体节点；(2) for...of 串行 await，N 个节点等待时间线性增长且无进度；(3) .catch(()=>{}) 静默吞错，部分失败时用户完全无感知。 | Dialog 确认时列出前 5 个节点名/MAC +「等 N 个」与不可逆警告；执行改 Promise.allSettled 并发（限并发≈5）；收集失败项，完成后用 aria-live 内联横幅回报「成功 X、失败 Y：mac1, mac2」；处理中 disable 批量条按钮并显示进度。 |
| 批量启用/禁用反馈与按钮态 | nodes.tsx:175-184, 392-409 (Power/PowerOff Buttons) | P1 | enable/disable 同样串行 await + 静默吞错，成功后只静默 loadNodes()，用户不知道哪些节点真正改变；无 processing/disabled 态，可重复点击。 | 复用 allSettled + aria-live 结果反馈；执行期间 disable 三个批量按钮并显示 spinner。enable/disable 可逆，无需 Dialog 二次确认，但需明确的完成反馈。 |
| Enabled 表单字段（Select 二选一） | nodes/detail.tsx:263-271 | P1 | 二元启用/禁用用 Select 下拉（多一步点击展开），且两个 SelectItem 文案都渲染同一个 t('enabled')（267-268），仅靠 ✓/✗ 字形区分——实际是 i18n key 缺失的功能性 bug，用户读屏时两项同名无法分辨。 | 换成 Switch：onCheckedChange:(checked)=>setEnabled(checked)，旁边标签显示「已启用 / 已禁用」（补两个独立 i18n key，如 enabledOn/enabledOff），符合 M3 toggle 规范且消除同名歧义。 |
| 表格行点击导航（onRowClick） | data-table.tsx:264-271 (TableRow onClick) | P1 | <tr> 仅绑 onClick，无 role/tabindex/键盘处理。键盘用户无法 Enter/Space 激活，读屏无法发现可点击（违反 WCAG 2.1.1）。 | TableRow 加 role='link' tabIndex={0} 与 onKeyDown（Enter/Space → preventDefault + onRowClick）；或把主列（note/hostname）渲染为真正的 <a>，行仅作视觉热区。同时补 hover:bg 提升与可选 chevron-right 作为导航 affordance。 |
| 图标按钮触控目标 + aria-label（行操作/刷新/分页） | nodes.tsx:238-241 (MoreHorizontal h-8=32px), nodes.tsx:297-304 (Refresh size-9=36px), data-table.tsx:299-317 (分页 h-9 w-9=36px) | P1 | 多处 icon-only 按钮低于 M3 48dp（行操作 32px、刷新 36px、分页 36px），且均无自定义 aria-label，读屏仅念默认图标名或泛化 button。 | 桌面下保持视觉尺寸但用 padding/touch-target 把可点区扩到≥44-48dp（或 @media (pointer:coarse) 升 h-11/w-11）；每个 icon-only 按钮补 aria-label（更多操作/重新加载/首页/上一页/下一页/末页），刷新加 Tooltip。 |
| 搜索输入框（无 label / 无防抖 / 无清空） | data-table.tsx:166-175 (Input) | P1 | Input 无关联 <label> 或 aria-label，读屏无可访问名；onChange 直接触发 useMemo 过滤，无防抖，节点多（1000+）时逐键重算卡顿；右侧无清空 X。 | 加 aria-label/sr-only label='搜索节点'；onSearchChange 加 debounce(300ms)；有值时在右侧显示清空按钮（X）一键复位。 |
| 可排序列头（缺 aria-sort） | data-table.tsx:229-243 (TableHead) | P1 | 排序方向仅靠 ArrowUp/ArrowDown 图标视觉传达，<th> 无 aria-sort，读屏无法感知当前排序列与方向；onClick 无键盘等价。 | 在可排序 <th> 加 aria-sort={sorted?'ascending'/'descending':'none'}，并加 role='button' + onKeyDown 支持键盘排序。 |
| 全选复选框（缺 indeterminate / 仅当前页） | data-table.tsx:107-113 (header Checkbox) | P2 | 表头 checkbox 只用 getIsAllPageRowsSelected()，部分选中时无 indeterminate 视觉/语义；且全选仅限当前页，多页时跨页操作易遗漏。 | checked 改用 indeterminate 表达：checked={getIsAllPageRowsSelected()? true : getIsSomeRowsSelected()? 'indeterminate' : false}；若业务允许跨页批量，在批量条加「选择全部 N 条」。 |
| 分页控件（无页大小选择 / 无区间 / 单页隐藏） | data-table.tsx:293-320 | P2 | 无每页条数选择器；左侧只显示『N rows』而非『显示 X–Y / 共 Z』；pageCount===1 时整条隐藏，无法感知结果范围；页码 span 变化无 aria-live 播报。 | 加 pageSize 下拉（20/50/100）；文案改『显示 X–Y / 共 Z 条』；页码区包 role=status aria-live='polite' aria-atomic 播报翻页。 |
| 动态计数 aria-live（已选数/行数/页码） | data-table.tsx:208-215 (selected badge), 295-297 (rows), 307-309 (page) | P2 | 选中数量、行数、当前页都是静态文本，筛选/选择/翻页变化时读屏无播报。 | 把这些计数包进 aria-live='polite' 区域（页码可用 role=status aria-atomic），让动态变化被宣告。 |
| 空态（无 CTA） | data-table.tsx:257-262 | P2 | 筛选无结果与真正无数据只换一行文字，filtered-empty 场景下无『清除筛选』出口，用户不知如何返回。 | filtered-empty 时显示『未找到匹配结果』+『清除筛选/重置搜索』按钮 CTA（清空 searchValue 与 statusFilter）；真正空数据保留引导文案。 |
| 状态过滤按钮组（缺 ARIA 语义） | nodes.tsx:366-390 | P2 | 4 个 <button> 选中态纯靠颜色，无 aria-pressed/aria-selected，外层无 role；读屏无法判断当前筛选。窄屏无 overflow 处理可能撑破。 | 作为 toggle 组：外层 role='group' aria-label='按状态筛选'，每个 button 加 aria-pressed={isActive}（若设计意图是 tab 则用 role=tablist/tab+aria-selected）；容器加 overflow-x-auto 防溢出。 |
| 导出 CSV 按钮（无反馈） | nodes.tsx:186-195 (exportCSV) + 289-296 (Button) | P2 | 点击后无 loading、无完成提示，大文件时页面看似无反应，用户可能重复点击。 | 点击临时 disable + spinner，完成后 aria-live 内联提示『已导出 N 条』。 |
