| 错误横幅（无 dismiss / 无 role） | nodes.tsx:341-345 | P2 | 错误用纯 <div>，无 role='alert'/aria-live='assertive'，读屏不即时播报；无关闭按钮，error 持续遮挡直到下次成功 loadNodes()。 | 加 role='alert'；提供 dismiss 关闭按钮，让用户保留查看已缓存列表。 |
| Weight 数字输入 | nodes/detail.tsx:284-292 | P2 | type='number' 在移动端/各浏览器渲染不一致（步进箭头有无不定），无法阻止非数字字符。 | 改 type='text' inputMode='numeric' pattern='[0-9]*'，或封装带步进按钮的 NumberInput；保留 min/max 校验。 |

#### pages/nodes/detail.tsx

- verdict: **major** · 控件数: 13 · P0/P1/P2: 1/2/10
- topPriority: enabled 字段用 Select 承载布尔量，且两个 SelectItem 文案都是「启用」（line 267-268 仅图标 ✓/✗ 不同），用户无法从文字区分开/关——控件选型错误 + 标签歧义双重缺陷，三份审查一致判 major。改为 Switch。

| 控件 | 位置 | 严重度 | 反模式 | 重设计方案 |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| enabled 启用/禁用 Select | line 263-271 | P0 | 布尔二元量用 Select dropdown 承载，需 展开→点击→关闭 三步切换；且两个 SelectItem 文案完全相同（'✓ 启用' / '✗ 启用'，line 267-268），仅图标区分，用户与屏幕阅读器都无法从文字判断哪项是关。底层值 '1'/'0' 经 SelectValue 朗读也非语义化。三份审查一致 major。 | 替换为 Switch：<div class="flex items-center gap-3"><Switch id="detail-enabled" checked={enabled} onCheckedChange={setEnabled} /><Label htmlFor="detail-enabled">{t('enabled')}</Label></div>。单击切换，Radix Switch 自带 role="switch"+aria-checked。移除歧义文案。 |
| weight 权重数字输入 | line 285-292 | P1 | onChange={(e)=>setWeight(Number(e.target.value))}：用户清空输入框时 Number('')=0，静默把权重重置为 0（数据损坏，line 291），用户无感知。同时 min/max 越界无 inline 反馈，0-10000 语义无说明。 | 改为保留空值：onChange={(e)=>setWeight(e.target.value===''?'':Number(e.target.value))}（weight state 改为 number\|'' 或独立字符串态）；下方加 helper text '权重范围 0–10000' 并 aria-describedby 关联；越界时显示 inline 错误而非依赖浏览器原生气泡。保存前校验非空且在范围内。 |
| saveError / saveSuccess 内联反馈条 | line 302-313 | P1 | 三问题叠加：(1) saveSuccess 无自动消失，永久驻留直到下次保存；(2) 两块均无 role/aria-live，屏幕阅读器不播报保存结果（违反 WCAG 4.1.3）；(3) 二者非互斥渲染，若状态管理出错可同时出现导致重叠。 | saveError 容器加 role="alert" aria-live="assertive"；saveSuccess 容器加 role="status" aria-live="polite"，并在 setSaveSuccess(true) 后用 setTimeout 3-4s 自动清除（配合淡出）。handleSave 已在开头清两态，保持互斥即可。若全站有 Snackbar 体系，优先提升为页面级 Snackbar。 |
| status=retired 破坏性状态变更 | line 273-281 + handleSave line 87-107 | P2 | 将节点标记为 retired（停止分配流量、近乎不可逆）与普通字段编辑走同一条静默保存路径，无任何二次确认，违反破坏性操作需确认的规范。 | 保存时若 status 由非 retired 变为 retired，弹 AlertDialog 确认：'确定将此节点标记为已退役？将停止向其分配流量。'，确认后再提交。 |
| LocationCombobox（地点选择）搜索匹配与硬编码占位符 | line 246-251；组件 components/ui/location-combobox.tsx line 54, 61 | P2 | CommandItem value={opt.label}（line 61）而非 opt.value：当两个 location 的 label 相同时 cmdk 按 value 去重/匹配会产生不确定行为；CommandInput placeholder 硬编码 '搜索...'（line 54）未走 i18n。 | CommandItem 改 value={opt.value \|\| opt.label}（保证唯一可搜）；若需按中文 label 搜索，用 cmdk 的 keywords={[opt.label]} 而非把 label 当 value。CommandInput placeholder 改为可传入 prop 或 t('searchPlaceholder')。 |
| 编辑区缺 <form> 包裹，Enter 不提交 | line 242-322 | P2 | note/weight/region 等受控输入未包在 <form> 中，用户在输入框按 Enter 不触发保存，违反表单交互预期；也无法利用浏览器对 number min/max 的原生校验。 | 用 <form onSubmit={(e)=>{e.preventDefault();handleSave();}}> 包裹编辑字段，保存 Button 设 type="submit"，让 Enter 提交且 number 输入参与原生校验。 |
| ProbeStatusCard 探针卡：静默失败 + 无刷新 | line 330-391（catch 空函数 line 340） | P2 | adminNodeStatus 失败时 catch(()=>{}) 完全吞掉，页面保留旧探针数据，用户不知数据是否过期或获取失败；仅在 mac 变化时拉一次，无手动刷新与轮询，无数据时间陈旧提示。 | 获取失败时展示 '无法获取探针状态' 的 disabled/idle chip 而非静默保旧值；CardHeader 右侧加 icon Button 手动刷新；可选每 30s 静默轮询，checked_at 距今超阈值时置灰提示。若加轮询，状态 chip 区加 aria-live="polite"。 |
| note 备注输入（潜在多行） | line 254-260 | P2 | 用单行 Input 承载备注，若内容较长换行体验差、无字符数提示。 | 若 note 允许长文本，改用 Textarea（已有原语）支持多行；如有后端长度上限，加 maxLength 与字符计数。 |
| CardTitle 标题语义 | 各 Card CardHeader（line 172 等）；组件 components/ui/card | P2 | CardTitle 渲染为 <div> 无 heading 语义，6+ 张卡片仅 1 个 h1，屏幕阅读器按 H 无法在各分区间导航，文档大纲缺失。 | CardTitle 渲染为语义化 <h2>（或支持 asChild/level prop）。本页各卡片标题统一 h2，使 hostname h1 → 分区 h2 形成清晰大纲。 |
| loading / error 全屏态无状态播报 | line 109-145 | P2 | loading 区与 error 区均无 role="status"/role="alert"，加载→完成、加载→失败的过渡不被辅助技术播报；spinner 与 animate-slide-up 无 reduced-motion 兜底。 | loading 容器加 role="status" aria-live="polite"，error 容器加 role="alert"。动效兜底见 prefers-reduced-motion 项。 |
| prefers-reduced-motion 全站缺失（本页 7 张卡 animate-slide-up + spinner 受影响） | styles/globals.css（影响 detail.tsx line 111/150/170-237/371 等） | P2 | globals.css 定义 animate-slide-up/fade-in/scale-in/spin 但无 @media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce) 兜底；本页每张卡 40-280ms 错峰滑入，对前庭敏感用户引发不适。 | 在 globals.css 末尾补：@media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce){*,*::before,*::after{animation-duration:.01ms!important;animation-iteration-count:1!important;transition-duration:.01ms!important;}}。全站一次性修复。 |
| status Select 当前态无视觉标识 | line 273-281 | P2 | 三态 status（控件选型本身正确）的选项与触发器无状态色点/Badge，与上方 assetInfo 卡的 status 展示不一致，当前态不易快速辨识。 | 在 SelectTrigger 与各 SelectItem 前嵌入状态色点/Chip（active=tertiary、maintenance=idle、retired=error），与探针/资产卡的 §10 语义色对齐。补 Label htmlFor 或 Trigger aria-labelledby 关联。 |

#### pages/node-status.tsx

- verdict: **major** · 控件数: 11 · P0/P1/P2: 0/2/9
- topPriority: 监控页数据只在 mount 加载一次(line 115),无轮询、无"最后更新时间",用户无法判断节点状态是否新鲜——这是状态监控页最致命的缺陷。应加 30s 轮询 + 显示 last-updated 时间戳。

| 控件 | 位置 | 严重度 | 反模式 | 重设计方案 |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| 页面数据加载策略 (无轮询) | lines 103-115, load() + useEffect([]) | P1 | useEffect 空依赖只在 mount 拉一次数据,节点状态监控页却没有自动轮询、没有'最后更新时间'、没有数据陈旧提示。用户盯着面板看到的可能是几小时前的状态,且毫无察觉。 | 在 useEffect 内加 setInterval(load, 30000) 并在 cleanup 中 clearInterval;新增 lastUpdated state(load 成功时 setLastUpdated(new Date())),在刷新按钮旁显示 '更新于 {相对时间}';轮询拉取走静默更新(不触发全表 loading 骨架,改用局部 inline spinner),避免每 30s 整表闪烁。可选:超过 N 分钟未成功刷新时给 chip 标 'stale'。 |
| Error banner (错误横幅) | lines 207-212 | P1 | 错误横幅仅靠文字传达,无 role="alert"/aria-live,屏幕阅读器在错误出现时不会自动播报;且无关闭按钮、无重试入口(只能靠 toolbar 的刷新),长错误文本可能溢出。 | 在 banner div 上加 role="alert"(隐式 assertive),确保错误即时播报;文本加 break-words 防溢出;在右侧加一个 ghost 图标按钮做 Retry(调用 load())或 dismiss。错误为页面级反馈,无需动共享原语。 |
| 动态区域 live-region (loading / empty / 统计计数) | lines 139-161 (stat chips), 253-265 (loading), 266-274 (empty) | P2 | loading 旋转器 aria-hidden 且容器无 role="status";空态、统计计数变化均无 aria-live。配合轮询后,屏幕阅读器对'加载中/无数据/计数变化'这些动态状态完全无感。 | loading 容器加 role="status" aria-label={tCommon('loading')};空态容器加 role="status" aria-live="polite";统计 chip 外层包 aria-live="polite"(轮询刷新时播报最新 online/offline 数)。 |
| Filter segment 三段筛选 (all/online/offline) | lines 170-192 | P2 | 原生 button+aria-pressed 硬凑分段控件:无 role="group"/aria-label;无左右箭头 roving-tabindex 键盘导航(不符合 ARIA radiogroup/segmented 模式);外层 overflow-hidden 会裁切 state-layer 的 hover/ripple;py-1.5 高度约 32px,低于 M3 48dp 触控目标。注:focus ring 已存在(line 179 ring-inset),无需补。 | 容器加 role="radiogroup" aria-label={t('filterLabel')};每个 button 改 role="radio" aria-checked + roving tabindex(选中项 tabIndex=0 其余 -1)+ onKeyDown 实现左右箭头切换;把 overflow-hidden 换成 rounded 子项各自裁切(或 isolate)以保留 ripple;移动端把 py-1.5 提到 min-h-12 满足 48dp。建议抽成 components/ui/segmented.tsx 复用。 |
| Empty state (筛选结果为空) | lines 266-274 | P2 | filter='online' 却无在线节点时,显示通用 t('noData'),与用户当前筛选意图矛盾(选了 online 却被告知'无数据'),且无清除筛选的快捷出口。 | 空态文案按 filter 上下文区分:filter!=='all' 时显示 '当前筛选无匹配节点' + 一个 'Clear filter' 文字按钮(onClick={() => setFilter('all')});filter==='all' 且 data 为空时才显示真正的 noData。 |
| Summary stat chips + 副标题 (布局跳动) | lines 128-136 (subtitle), 139-161 (chips) | P2 | Offline 卡仅在 offlineCount>0 时渲染(line 154),节点全上线/某个掉线时工具栏水平晃动;副标题在 data 加载前为空字符串(line 134),数据到达后内容区整体下移(CLS);Total 用 border、Online/Offline 用 colored container,视觉处理不一致。 | 三个统计卡始终渲染,Offline 在 count=0 时用 bg-muted + text-muted-foreground 表示零态,消除晃动;副标题加载前显示静态占位('Monitoring nodes…')或 skeleton,避免 CLS;统一三卡视觉(全部 colored container 或全部 border)。 |

| PctBar / Latency 阈值与色彩语义 | lines 66-93 (pctColor/PctBar), 304-308 (latency inline) | P2 | 负载阈值 70/90 与 latency 200ms 警告值散落在多处硬编码(latency 阈值还内联在 render line 305),不一致且难维护;高/中负载仅靠颜色区分,屏幕阅读器只读到数字,拿不到'高负载'语义。 | 提取模块级常量 CPU_WARN/CPU_CRIT(70/90)与 LATENCY_WARNING_MS(200)并复用;PctBar 给数值 span 加 aria-label={`${pct(v)}${v>=90?' 高负载':v>=70?' 中等负载':''}`},为色彩语义提供文本替代。理想情况阈值由后端告警配置下发,保持前后端一致。 |
| Data Table 排序 / 分页 / 表格语义 | lines 220-317, Table | P2 | 数值列(CPU/Mem/Disk/Latency/Uptime)不可排序、表头无 aria-sort;全量一次渲染无分页(当前生产仅 ~11 节点风险低,但节点增长后首屏会卡);表格无可排序状态指示。 | 为数值列增加点击排序,表头按当前排序设 aria-sort=ascending\|descending\|none;节点数显著增长时(>50)引入客户端分页(每页 20-50)或虚拟滚动。优先做排序+aria-sort,分页随规模再上。 |

| 动画 prefers-reduced-motion 兜底 | lines 126/129/140/280 (animate-slide-up/fade-in 含 i*30ms 逐行延迟), 259/201 (animate-spin) | P2 | 逐行 animation-delay(i*30ms)叠加 slide-up/fade-in 与 spin,均无 prefers-reduced-motion 兜底,对开启'减少动画'偏好的用户(含前庭功能敏感)造成干扰。 | 在全局样式加 @media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce){ .animate-slide-up,.animate-fade-in{animation:none} .animate-spin{animation-duration:.001ms} },尊重系统偏好;大列表逐行 stagger 在 reduced-motion 下直接禁用。 |

#### pages/gateway.tsx

- verdict: **major** · 控件数: 13 · P0/P1/P2: 1/4/8
- topPriority: 反馈 Snackbar(lines 243-259)是全页最高优先级:三个视角一致判 major。它同时存在三个缺陷——无关闭按钮、无自动消失(永驻到下次保存才被覆盖)、且没有 aria-live/role,导致屏幕阅读器用户在保存成功/失败时得不到任何播报。这是唯一对所有用户(视觉+读屏)都构成功能性反馈缺失的问题,应最先修。

| 控件 | 位置 | 严重度 | 反模式 | 重设计方案 |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Feedback Snackbar (success/error status div) | gateway.tsx:243-259 | P0 | 三视角一致判 major。该状态条既不可关闭、也不自动消失——一旦出现会持续到下一次 patchField 才被 setFeedback(null) 覆盖,过时消息可滞留整个 session。更严重的是它只是个带样式的 <div>,无 role / aria-live,屏幕阅读器在保存成功或失败时完全无播报。这违背 transient feedback 最佳实践和 WCAG 4.1.3 Status Messages。 | 重构为真正的 Snackbar 行为:(1) useEffect 监听 feedback,setTimeout 4000ms 后 setFeedback(null),return 清理 timer(成功态自动消失;错误态可延长或保留)。(2) 错误态加一个 X 关闭图标按钮(用 Button size="icon-xs" variant="ghost")。(3) 容器加 role={feedback.kind==='err' ? 'alert' : 'status'} 与 aria-live={feedback.kind==='err' ? 'assertive' : 'polite'} aria-atomic="true"。建议长期抽成共享 Snackbar/Toast 原语,因为该模式在多页复用。 |
| Enabled Switch (per-row toggle) | gateway.tsx:387-392 | P1 | 冲突仲裁:Lens C 判 ok,但 Lens B 判 major、Lens A 判 minor,以严判为准。开关状态仅靠颜色(绿/灰 + thumb 位置)传达,违反 WCAG 1.4.1 Use of Color;且 aria-label 取列头文案 t('colEnabled'),读屏用户无法得知当前 ON/OFF。 | 在 Switch 内加视觉隐藏的状态文本 <span className="sr-only">{enabled ? t('switchEnabled') : t('switchDisabled')}</span>,并将 aria-label 改为状态感知字符串 aria-label={enabled ? t('switchEnabled') : t('switchDisabled')}。若希望全站一致,可把 sr-only 状态文本内建进 Switch 原语(接受 onLabel/offLabel 可选 props)。 |
| Error banner (load failure) | gateway.tsx:227-233 | P1 | 冲突仲裁:Lens A 判 ok、Lens C minor、Lens B major,取严判。动态出现的加载错误没有 role="alert"/aria-live,读屏不播报;且无重试入口,用户只能靠刷新按钮恢复。 | 容器加 role="alert" aria-live="assertive" aria-atomic="true"。在消息末尾追加一个文本按钮(Button variant="link" size="sm")调用 loadNodes() 做 Retry。错误为持续性状态,不要自动消失。 |
| GatewayTable horizontal overflow / responsive layout | gateway.tsx:322 (容器), 323-478 (表) | P1 | 6 列含两个 Select + 一个多选触发器,外层是 overflow-hidden。窄于 ~900px 时内容被裁切,无横向滚动提示、无移动端卡片化、无列优先级折叠。违反审查范围内明确要求的「移动端可达性 / M3 触控目标 ≥48dp」。 | 最低限度:外层 div 改 overflow-x-auto 并加边缘阴影提示可滚动。推荐:在 <md 断点切换为卡片布局——每个节点一张卡,Hostname/Location 作标题,Enabled/Direction/Mode/Upstreams 控件纵向堆叠,保证每个控件触控目标 ≥48dp。 |
| UpstreamMultiSelect listbox (checkbox 选项列表) | gateway.tsx:88-118 | P1 | 手写 <div role="listbox" aria-multiselectable> 缺键盘导航:Tab 落到首项后即退出 listbox,无 ArrowUp/Down 移动、无 Space/Enter 切换(Lens C)。同时 ARIA 不完整(Lens B):<label role="option"> 无 id、长列表无 aria-setsize/aria-posinset。 | 首选:用 components/ui/command 的 Command/CommandList/CommandItem 重写选项列表,自带方向键导航与过滤搜索,选中态用 Checkbox 或勾标显示。若保留自写 listbox:加 onKeyDown 处理 ArrowUp/Down 移动 roving focus、Space/Enter toggle;每个 <label role="option"> 加 id={mac};列表 >10 项时加 aria-setsize/aria-posinset。 |
| Refresh icon button (header) | gateway.tsx:196-206 | P2 | 合并 Lens A(36px 触控靶 < M3 48dp)与 Lens C(手写 <button> 复制了 state-layer/ripple/focus-ring,绕过 Button 原语契约)。Lens B 判 ok。 | 替换为 <Button variant="outline" size="icon-lg" onClick={loadNodes} disabled={loading} aria-label={tCommon('refresh')}><RefreshCw className={loading ? 'animate-spin' : ''} /></Button>。注意:Button 原语最大 icon 尺寸 icon-lg = size-11(44px),仍未达 48dp;若严格要求 48dp 触控靶,需在 button.tsx 新增一个 icon-xl(size-12)variant。 |
| UpstreamMultiSelect trigger (combobox 按钮) | gateway.tsx:66-83 | P2 | 合并三视角 minor:(A)mode 从 auto 切到 manual 后触发器出现但无引导,placeholder 读起来像禁用态;(B)listbox 无 aria-describedby 关联触发器用途说明;(C)无搜索过滤,节点多时只能滚动 + label 截断无法看全。 | (1) 给 listbox 加 aria-describedby 指向触发器(已有 useId 的 listboxId 可复用,或新增描述 span)。(2) 节点可能 >10 时配合上一条改用 Command 原语,内置搜索 CommandInput。(3) 触发器加 Tooltip 显示完整 label 全文。(4) 可选:切到 manual 后用 useEffect 给触发器加 3s 高亮/pulse 引导。 |
| Enabled Switch — 关闭网关无确认 / 乐观更新无 Undo | gateway.tsx:162-178 (patchField), 386-393 (Switch) | P2 | 合并 Lens A(乐观更新即时提交、误触无法回滚)与 Lens C(关闭网关这一系统级动作无确认、无上游影响提示)。仲裁:为每次 toggle 弹确认 Dialog 过重,会拖慢高频内联编辑。 | 采用「Snackbar + Undo」而非确认弹窗:保存成功后在反馈 Snackbar 内提供 Undo 动作按钮,调用反向 patch(把 gateway_enabled 切回原值 / 还原 Select)。仅对「关闭一个当前被其他节点引用为上游的网关」这类有下游影响的场景,额外在 Undo 旁提示受影响节点数。 |

#### pages/lines.tsx

- verdict: **major** · 控件数: 16 · P0/P1/P2: 0/3/13
- topPriority: Replace the native window.confirm()/window.alert() used for the destructive Delete action (and its failure path) with a themed alertdialog-style Dialog: it is the single most-agreed major issue across all three lenses, breaks design-system/dark-mode consistency, has no ARIA roles, and surfaces failures via an un-styled browser alert instead of inline error state.

| 控件 | 位置 | 严重度 | 反模式 | 重设计方案 |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Delete action confirmation + failure feedback | lines.tsx:142-150 (handleDelete), trigger button 459-466 | P1 | Destructive delete uses native window.confirm() at line 143 and reports failure via window.alert() at line 148. Bypasses the M3 Dialog system entirely: no dark-mode theming, no ARIA alertdialog role, OS-dependent keyboard behavior, and the failure message never reaches the page's inline error pattern. | Add a dedicated confirmation Dialog (role alertdialog) that names the line being deleted, uses error-role styling on the confirm button, and offers explicit Cancel + Delete buttons. On failure, set an inline error state (mirror the existing createError/editError/saveNodesError pattern) instead of alert(). Disable the confirm button while the delete is in-flight to prevent double-submit. |
| Reset Token confirmation + failure feedback | lines.tsx:216-224 (handleResetToken), trigger button 427-439 | P1 | Token reset uses window.confirm() at line 217 and window.alert() at line 222. Same skin-deep-M3 problem as delete: native dialogs bypass theming/ARIA, and the irreversible token invalidation gives no in-app context about consequences (existing subscription links will break). | Replace with a confirmation Dialog that explains the consequence (existing sub-links stop working) and names the line. Medium-severity recoverable-by-re-share action, so a clear warning Dialog is sufficient (no name-typing gate needed). Route failures to an inline error state, not alert(). |
| Edit dialog — Status enable/disable toggle | lines.tsx:614-626 | P1 | Custom <button> styled as a pill toggle. Has no role='switch' and no aria-checked — on/off state is conveyed only through CSS color (bg-md-tertiary-container vs bg-muted), so screen readers hear a generic button and cannot perceive or announce the toggled state. The shipped Switch primitive (Radix-backed, M3-correct, accessible) is unused. | Replace the custom button with <Switch checked={editEnabled} onCheckedChange={setEditEnabled} />. The save-on-submit semantic is preserved (Switch just drives editEnabled); Switch supplies role=switch, aria-checked, keyboard handling, focus ring, and correct M3 sizing automatically. |
| All dialog error messages + page-level error banner | lines.tsx:293-301 (page banner), 532-537 (createError), 628-633 (editError), 706-711 (saveNodesError) | P2 | Every error <p>/<div> uses bg-md-error-container styling but has no role='alert', no aria-live, and no id. When error state flips after an async failure, screen readers do not announce it — the failure is visual-only. | Add role='alert' aria-live='assertive' to each error container, and give each a unique id so inputs can reference it via aria-describedby. The page banner (293-301) should also get role='alert'. |
| Note input fields (Create + Edit dialogs) | lines.tsx:525-530 (create), 606-610 (edit) | P2 | Multi-line note content uses single-line <Input>, which truncates visually and is awkward for sentence-length notes. | Swap both note Inputs for the Textarea primitive. Keep the same value/onChange wiring; add a sensible default rows count. |
| Node Edit dialog — node selection checkboxes | lines.tsx:690-695 | P2 | Native <input type='checkbox'> styled with accent-md-primary, instead of the project Checkbox primitive. Inconsistent focus state and styling versus the rest of the app; each checkbox's accessible name relies on adjacent bracketed-location text rather than an explicit label. | Replace native inputs with <Checkbox checked onCheckedChange>. Give each row an explicit accessible name combining hostname + location (+ mac) so AT reads a consistent label. |
| Custom <button> elements (header, table-row actions, dialog footers) | lines.tsx:259-274, 276-288, 400-425, 427-439, 445-451, 452-458, 459-466, 540-557, 636-653, 714-731 | P2 | Buttons are hand-rolled with repeated state-layer/focus-ring className blocks instead of the Button primitive, despite Button being imported. Inconsistent and error-prone (each instance re-implements focus/disabled styling). | Migrate to <Button> with the appropriate variant (filled for primary Save/Create, outlined for Refresh/Cancel, text for row actions). Preserve the copiedId icon/text swap on the copy button and the error-color styling on Delete via the destructive variant. |
| Node Edit dialog — search input | lines.tsx:672-677 | P2 | filteredNodes recomputes synchronously on every keystroke with no debounce (janky for 100+ node lists), there is no clear (X) affordance, and the zero-result empty state (681-683) has no aria-live so filtering-to-empty is silent to AT. | Wrap the filter value in useDeferredValue or a 300ms debounce; add a clear button shown when nodeSearch is non-empty that resets and refocuses; add role='status' aria-live='polite' to the empty-state <p>. |
| Edit dialog — Save button enablement | lines.tsx:644-646 | P2 | Save is disabled only on `editing`, not on empty name. Create's Save correctly guards `!createName.trim()`, so the two dialogs are inconsistent and Edit allows a wasted server round-trip that fails. | Add the same guard: disabled={editing \|\| !editName.trim()}. |
| Region input fields (Create + Edit dialogs) | lines.tsx:502-507 (create), 585-589 (edit) | P2 | Region is free-text in both dialogs. If region is a finite vocabulary, free text invites inconsistent values (us-east / US-East / US East) that fragment grouping/filtering. Verdict was split across lenses because the vocabulary size is unconfirmed. | Confirm whether region is a bounded set. If yes, replace both Inputs with a searchable combobox/select fed by the known regions (apply identically to Create and Edit). If region is genuinely free-form, keep Input but normalize on submit (trim + case policy). |
| Copy Link button — success feedback | lines.tsx:400-425 | P2 | The 2-second 'copied' confirmation is icon/text/color swap only — no aria-live announcement, so screen-reader users get no confirmation the link was copied. | Add a visually-hidden aria-live='polite' region (or role='status' on the button while in copied state) that announces the copied confirmation when copiedId changes. |
| Required-field indicators on Name (Create + Edit) | lines.tsx:487-496 (create), 571-579 (edit) | P2 | Name is required (Create's Save disables on empty) but the label carries no visual required marker and inputs lack aria-required, so users scanning the form get no cue and AT does not announce the requirement. | Add a required indicator to the Name label (asterisk or required-dot consistent with the design system) and aria-required='true' on the inputs. |
| Node Edit dialog — selection summary + bulk actions | lines.tsx:678-705 | P2 | A potentially long checkbox list with no visible selection count and no Select All / Deselect All shortcut; Save is also enabled even when no change was made versus the initial selection. | Add a 'N of M selected' counter above the list and Select All / Deselect All link-actions. Capture initial selectedMacs on open and disable Save when the set is unchanged. |
| Lines table semantics | lines.tsx:306-316 | P2 | Table has no <caption> and the column <th> cells lack scope='col'; if sorting is added later there is no aria-sort plan. | Add a caption (visually-hidden is fine) naming the table, and emit scope='col' on header cells. Ideally fix this once in the shared Table/TableHead primitive so all pages benefit. |
| Display Order numeric input (Create + Edit) | lines.tsx:513-519 (create), 595-600 (edit) | P2 | type='number' inputs have no min/step constraints; invalid entries are silently coerced via parseInt(...)\|\|0, masking mistakes from the user. | Add min='0' step='1' to constrain input, and surface an inline hint if the value is non-numeric rather than silently defaulting to 0. |
| Per-row action button group (Edit / Edit Nodes / Delete) | lines.tsx:442-469 | P2 | Three text action buttons per row (plus Copy/Reset-Token in the adjacent column) crowd narrow/mobile viewports and risk horizontal overflow; touch targets at px-3 py-1.5 text-xs are also below the M3 48dp minimum. | On small screens, collapse secondary actions (Edit, Edit Nodes) into an overflow/kebab menu, keeping Delete distinct. Ensure each actionable item meets the 48dp touch target. |

#### pages/users.tsx

- verdict: **major** · 控件数: 12 · P0/P1/P2: 2/4/6
- topPriority: 把 handleDelete 的 window.confirm 换成页面内 Dialog 确认（destructive variant + 显示用户名 + 不可撤销文案），这是「换皮没换交互」最刺眼的遗留，且破坏性操作缺少受设计系统控制的确认流程。

| 控件 | 位置 | 严重度 | 反模式 | 重设计方案 |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| 删除用户确认 (handleDelete) | pages/users.tsx:124-135 | P0 | 破坏性操作用原生 window.confirm()：阻塞主线程、无焦点 trap、样式脱离 M3 设计系统、文案锁死「确定/取消」无法表达后果，且无法显示受影响用户名。三份审查一致判 major。 | 新增 confirm 状态（如 deleteTarget: AdminUser \| null），点删除时 setDeleteTarget(u) 打开一个复用现有 Dialog 的确认弹窗。标题「删除用户」，正文「确定删除 {username} 吗？此操作不可撤销，该用户将立即失去访问权限。」取消按钮 outline，确认按钮用 Button variant=destructive。该确认弹窗禁用点击遮罩关闭（onPointerDownOutside preventDefault），与低风险表单弹窗区分。确认后才调用 adminDeleteUser。 |
| 编辑角色弹窗 — 自定义 div+svg 复选框列表 | pages/users.tsx:566-605 | P0 | 用 label + 隐藏 sr-only input + 手绘 svg 勾选模拟复选框，未复用已存在的 Checkbox 原语。真实缺陷（仲裁后修正夸大表述）：sr-only input 仍可 Tab/Space 操作，但视觉勾选框无 focus-visible 焦点环（WCAG 2.4.7 失败）；角色 description 未通过 aria-describedby 关联；与全站 checkbox 风格/无障碍实现不一致、代码重复。 | 改用 <Checkbox checked={checked} onCheckedChange={() => toggleRole(r.name)} id={`role-${r.id}`} />，外层 label htmlFor 指向它；description 段落给 id={`role-desc-${r.id}`} 并在 Checkbox 上加 aria-describedby。保留行级 hover/选中底色样式（套在包裹 label 上即可）。Checkbox 原语自带 focus-visible:ring-2，焦点可见问题随之解决。 |
| 表格行图标按钮 ×3（编辑角色 / 改密 / 删除） | pages/users.tsx:372-381, 382-391, 395-406 | P1 | 两处事实纠正：(1) 按钮只有 title，并无 aria-label（审查1、2 误称已有 aria-label）；(2) 尺寸 h-8 w-8 = 32px，违反本页 M3 触控目标 ≥48dp 契约（注：WCAG 2.5.8 AA 下限是 24px，故这是 M3 契约违规而非 AA 失败）。icon-only 按钮缺可访问名是真实 4.1.2 问题。 | 三个按钮改用 Button asChild size="icon-lg"（size-11=44px，最接近 48dp 的现成档位；如需精确 48 用 min-h-12 min-w-12 覆盖）。每个显式加 aria-label（editRoles / changePassword / deleteUser），title 可保留作 tooltip 但不可作为唯一可访问名。删除按钮可将默认色调向 error 倾斜以体现 destructive 语义，但属次要。若担心三个 48px 按钮在窄行挤占空间，可收进 dropdown-menu 的「更多操作」溢出菜单。 |
| 表单 Label 与 Input 的程序化关联（用户名/密码/新密码） | pages/users.tsx:432-441, 444-454, 514-524 | P1 | Label 无 htmlFor、Input 无 id，二者无关联，屏幕阅读器无法朗读字段用途（WCAG 1.3.1 / 4.1.2）。事实纠正：Input 原语已 {...props} 透传，id 直接可用，无需改原语（审查2「需改原语」错误）。 | 给每个 Input 加唯一 id（new-username / new-password / changepwd-password），对应 Label 加 htmlFor。顺带补 autoComplete：用户名 autoComplete="username"，两个密码字段 autoComplete="new-password"，提升密码管理器集成。 |
| 状态横幅（error / success banner） | pages/users.tsx:250-263 | P1 | 两类问题合并：(a) 无 role/aria-live，动态出现的成败消息不会被屏幕阅读器播报（4.1.3）；(b) 无自动消失/手动关闭，success 长期占位；(c) loadData 只 setError('') 不 setSuccess('')，刷新后上次成功提示残留。 | error 横幅加 role="alert" aria-live="assertive"；success 横幅加 role="status" aria-live="polite"。success 设置 4-5s 后自动清空（useEffect + setTimeout，卸载清理）。loadData 起始处同时 setSuccess('') 清残留。error 保留直至下次操作或用户主动关闭（可加 X 按钮）。 |
| 用户表格 — 搜索 / 筛选 / 分页 | pages/users.tsx:266-415 | P1 | 无搜索框、无角色筛选、无分页，全部用户单页渲染。审查1判 major、审查3判 minor。仲裁：管理员用户表通常规模有限，定为 P1——优先加搜索/筛选，分页按实际规模决定。 | toolbar 内（紧邻 refresh）加按 username 实时过滤的搜索 Input（debounce 300ms）；可选加角色筛选 Select。搜索/筛选状态写入 URL query params，刷新不丢。当用户数超过阈值（如 50）再引入分页或虚拟滚动，不必一次性上。 |
| 创建用户弹窗 — 关闭后表单状态未重置 | pages/users.tsx:418, 475-483 | P2 | handleCreate 成功才重置 newUsername/newPassword/newRole；点 Cancel 或遮罩/Esc 关闭不重置，下次打开残留上次输入。（改密、角色弹窗已在 openPwd/openRoles 里重置，无此问题。） | 改用 Dialog onOpenChange：open===false 时统一清空 newUsername/newPassword/newRole（并清 inline 校验态）。Cancel 按钮走同一 onOpenChange 路径即可。 |
| 创建用户弹窗 — 用户名/密码即时校验 | pages/users.tsx:435-441, 447-454 | P2 | 仅靠禁用 Save 防空提交，格式/长度/重复校验全部推迟到提交后后端返回；用户填写期间无任何反馈，也无密码强度/规则提示。 | onBlur（或 debounce onChange）做基础客户端校验（非空、最小长度、字符集），不合法时 Input 加 aria-invalid 并在下方显示 inline error。密码字段在 Label 旁注明规则（如「至少 8 位，含字母和数字」），可选加轻量强度条（用辅助文本颜色，不必新增控件）。 |
| 三个弹窗缺少 DialogDescription | pages/users.tsx:419-429, 501-511, 554-564 | P2 | DialogContent 只有 DialogTitle 无 DialogDescription，Radix 会发出缺 aria-describedby 警告，且对话框无补充说明（1.3.1）。 | 每个弹窗在 DialogHeader 内加一个 DialogDescription（已从 dialog.tsx 导出）。内容自解释的可放 sr-only 简述（如「创建一个新的后台用户账户」）。 |
| 改密操作 — 无风险提示 | pages/users.tsx:382-391, 500-550 | P2 | 改密不可撤销且会迫使目标用户重新登录，但点按钮直接开弹窗、弹窗内也无任何警示。 | 在改密弹窗标题下用 DialogDescription 加一句提示：「重置 {username} 的密码后，该用户当前会话将失效，需用新密码重新登录。」无需二次确认弹窗，文案到位即可。 |
| 刷新按钮 — 视觉权重/控件选型 | pages/users.tsx:222-233 | P2 | 次要操作用 border+bg-card+state-layer 实现，与主操作 Create User 视觉权重接近，破坏 M3 强调层级（审查3）。属控件强调级别/IA，不属纯配色，故纳入。 | 降级为 text/ghost 按钮：去掉 border 与 bg-card，用 text-muted-foreground + hover 态 state layer，与 Create 的 filled 主操作拉开层级。建议直接换用 Button variant="ghost" 保持一致。 |
| 编辑角色弹窗 — 批量全选/清空 + 空选保护 | pages/users.tsx:565-606, 176-177 | P2 | 角色多时需逐个点选，缺全选/清空快捷操作（审查3）；handleSaveRoles 在空选择时静默 return，虽 Save 已 disabled 但键盘 Enter 极端路径无反馈。 | 角色列表顶部加「全选 / 清空」两个 text button。handleSaveRoles 空选择分支改为给出可见提示（toast 或 inline「请至少选择一个角色」）而非静默 return。 |

#### pages/roles.tsx

- verdict: **major** · 控件数: 14 · P0/P1/P2: 0/4/10
- topPriority: Replace the custom 16px checkbox with the existing Radix Checkbox primitive (size-[18px], real focus/keyboard/ARIA), and give the error/success banners aria-live so screen-reader users are not left with silent feedback. These are the two changes that fix correctness, not polish.

| 控件 | 位置 | 严重度 | 反模式 | 重设计方案 |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Permission checkbox (custom 16px span + sr-only native input) | lines 227-261 (label), 232-250 (custom visual span), 251-257 (sr-only input) | P1 | Hand-rolled checkbox: a size-4 (16px) visual <span> driven by a className="sr-only" native <input>. The project already ships an accessible Radix Checkbox at components/ui/checkbox.tsx sized size-[18px] with focus-visible ring, disabled state, and scale-in indicator. The custom version is undersized (16 vs M3 18px), reimplements checked styling by hand, and the visual span gets no focus ring (focus lands on an invisible sr-only input). Arbitration: Review B's claim that label/input are unassociated is wrong — the input is wrapped by the label so activation works — but the duplicate hand-built visual is still the defect. | Drop the custom <span> + sr-only <input>. Render <Checkbox checked={checked} onCheckedChange={() => canWrite && togglePerm(rid, p.slug)} disabled={!canWrite} /> inside the label, keep the text span as the label content. This restores correct 18px sizing, visible focus ring, keyboard Space/Enter, and proper data-[state=checked] styling for free. |
| Error / Success status banners | lines 134-139 (error), 140-145 (success) | P1 | Both banners are plain <div>s with no live-region semantics, so a screen-reader user gets zero announcement when a save fails or succeeds (WCAG 4.1.3). Additionally the success banner never clears on its own — it is only replaced when the next handleSave sets loading/error, so it lingers indefinitely after a successful save. | Add role="alert" (assertive) to the error banner and role="status" aria-live="polite" to the success banner. Auto-dismiss the success banner with a useEffect: when success is set, setTimeout(() => setSuccess(''), 5000) with cleanup. Keep the error banner until resolved but add a dismiss affordance. Do NOT migrate to a 'Radix Toast primitive' — none exists in components/ui; this is an in-place fix matching the gateway.tsx banner pattern. |
| Per-role Save button (no dirty/diff awareness) | lines 200-209 (Save button), 26/74-81 (editPerms state, togglePerm), 83-102 (handleSave) | P1 | There is no dirty tracking: the Save button is always enabled (only blocked while saving), gives no signal of whether anything changed, and the count badge shows only the live edit count with no reference to the saved state. A user cannot tell which roles have pending edits, and after handleSave triggers loadData() any concurrently-edited (unsaved) role's edits are silently reset because editPerms is rebuilt from the server. | Compute isDirty[rid] by comparing editPerms[rid] against the role's saved Set (role.permissions). Disable Save when not dirty, and show an 'unsaved' dot on dirty cards. In the count badge show saved→new delta when dirty (e.g. 12 -> 15). After a successful save, refresh only that role rather than reloading every card, so other in-progress edits are not clobbered. |
| Destructive permission change (removing own role:write / last admin) | lines 83-102 (handleSave) — no guard | P1 | handleSave writes permissions with no confirmation. A user can remove role:write (or the last role granting it) from their own effective role and instantly lock themselves out of this page, with no warning and no undo. | Before submitting, detect if the new permission set removes the current user's own role:write (or role:read) and require an explicit confirm dialog ('You are removing your own write access') using the existing dialog.tsx. Treat this as the destructive-action confirmation guardrail, not a generic toast. |
| Refresh button (bare <button>) | lines 123-130 | P2 | Bare <button> with copied state-layer/ripple classes instead of the imported Button primitive, so it drifts from the shared variant system. It already has a visible text child {tCommon('refresh')}, so it DOES have an accessible name — Review A/B's 'add aria-label' is unnecessary. | Use <Button variant="outline" onClick={loadData} disabled={loading}><RefreshCw className={loading ? 'animate-spin' : ''} />{tCommon('refresh')}</Button>. Note: there is no 'tonal' variant and no leftIcon prop (Review C is wrong); icon is passed as a child and the variant for a neutral reload is 'outline' (or 'secondary' for tonal emphasis). |
| Per-role Save button (bare <button> styling) | lines 201-208 | P2 | Bare <button> re-implements the filled/elevation-1/hover:elevation-2 styling that Button variant="default" already provides, duplicating focus and disabled handling by hand. | Use <Button variant="default" onClick={() => handleSave(role)} disabled={saving === rid}><Save className={saving === rid ? 'animate-pulse' : ''} />{saving === rid ? tCommon('saving') : tCommon('save')}</Button>. |
| Role card container (bare <div>) | lines 182-186 (card), 188 (header), 213 (body) — Card/CardHeader/CardContent imported but unused | P2 | Card, CardHeader, CardContent are imported (line 10) but the role card is a hand-built <div className="bg-card border rounded-xl">, bypassing the shared Card structure and its consistent padding/elevation. | Wrap each role in <Card> with CardHeader for the title/badge/Save row and CardContent for the permission grid, so future Card changes propagate and structure is semantic. |
| Permission count badge (bare <span>) | lines 196-198 | P2 | A bare pill <span> showing only currentSet.size reimplements the Badge primitive and announces to screen readers as a context-free number ('12'). Badge is imported (line 11) but unused. | Use <Badge> with the number plus an sr-only unit, e.g. <Badge>{currentSet.size}<span className="sr-only"> {t('permissions')}</span></Badge>. When dirty, render the saved->new delta here. |
| Loading spinner (no accessible name) | lines 148-173 | P2 | The CSS circular-progress SVG has no accessible name and the 'Loading...' text is decorative-only, not tied to a live region, so assistive tech gets no busy/loading signal. | Wrap the spinner block in role="status" aria-live="polite" and add a <span className="sr-only">{tCommon('loading')}</span> so the loading state is announced once. |
| Permission label row touch target | lines 227-230 (label: px-2 py-1.5) | P2 | Arbitration of A vs B: the full label row is the click target (good), but py-1.5 + text-sm yields a ~32px row height — below the M3 48dp minimum. Review A's '~48px, ok' is incorrect; Review B fixated on the 16px box instead of the actual row. | Raise the row to >=48dp on touch (e.g. py-2.5 / min-h-[44px], or min-h-12 on coarse pointers) so the whole label meets M3 touch sizing once the Checkbox primitive supplies the 18px control. |
| Empty state (roles.length === 0) | lines 177-273 (role list renders nothing when empty) | P2 | When there are no roles the content area renders an empty div with no message, indistinguishable from a load glitch. | Add an explicit empty state (icon + 'No roles configured' copy, plus a Create CTA when canWrite) so the blank state reads as intentional. |
| Permission group hidden when empty | line 217 (if groupPerms.length === 0 return null) | P2 | A group with zero matching permissions is silently dropped, so 'API returned nothing' looks identical to 'group legitimately empty'. | Only hide a group when allPerms is non-empty; if allPerms loaded but a known PERM_GROUPS key has no slugs, render a muted 'No permissions in this group' line. |
| Unauthorized redirect (role:read missing) | lines 40-44 | P2 | Users lacking role:read are router.replace'd to /dashboard with no explanation and no focus management on the SPA transition. | Show a brief 'Access denied — role:read required' message (or a /403 view) before/while redirecting, and move focus to the heading on navigation so screen-reader users are not stranded. |
| Global animations ignore prefers-reduced-motion | roles.tsx animate-fade-in/slide-up/spin/pulse (lines 109,128,135,141,149,153,184,206); checkbox.tsx animate-scale-in | P2 | styles/globals.css has no prefers-reduced-motion handling, so every animate-* utility runs regardless of the user's OS motion setting (WCAG 2.3.3). | Add a global @media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce) rule in globals.css that neutralizes animation/transition durations, so all animate-* utilities (including the Checkbox indicator) are quieted in one place. |

#### pages/audit-logs.tsx

- verdict: **major** · 控件数: 16 · P0/P1/P2: 3/6/7
- topPriority: P0: 四个筛选字段(原生 select + 3 个 Input)全部缺少 label↔控件的 htmlFor/id 关联,屏幕阅读器无法确定字段含义(WCAG 1.3.1)。这是全页最高优先级、且修复成本最低的无障碍阻断项。

| 控件 | 位置 | 严重度 | 反模式 | 重设计方案 |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| 筛选区四个表单字段的 label 关联缺失(Audit Action select / Username / From / To) | lines 140-187(每个 <label> 无 htmlFor,对应 select/Input 无 id 也无 aria-label) | P0 | label 与控件仅靠视觉邻近,无 htmlFor/id 配对,也无 aria-label。屏幕阅读器读到控件时不会播报字段名;点击 label 也不会聚焦控件。违反 WCAG 1.3.1 / 4.1.2。三份审查一致定级 major。 | 为每个控件加稳定 id(filter-action / filter-username / filter-from / filter-to),对应 <label htmlFor>。若改用下方的 Select 原语,则给 SelectTrigger 加 id + aria-labelledby 指向 label。placeholder 不得充当唯一标签。 |
| Error banner 无 live region | lines 208-213 | P0 | setError() 注入的错误文本所在 <div> 没有 role="alert" / aria-live,动态出现的错误对屏幕阅读器完全不可见(WCAG 4.1.3)。同时无 dismiss、无重试 CTA,错误只能靠下次请求清除。 | 给该 div 加 role="alert" aria-live="assertive"。banner 内追加一个 text/ghost 的「重试」按钮调用 loadLogs(page),并提供关闭按钮调用 setError('')。这是 M3 alert-with-action 模式。 |

#### pages/customers.tsx

- verdict: **major** · 控件数: 16 · P0/P1/P2: 1/5/10
- topPriority: P0: 邮箱搜索每次按键都触发整轮 API 请求 (line 195 → 108 的 useEffect)。加 300–400ms 防抖，停止输入后才发请求。三个视角一致判定为本页最严重交互缺陷。

| 控件 | 位置 | 严重度 | 反模式 | 重设计方案 |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Email search Input (debounce) | pages/customers.tsx:192-198 + loadCustomers useEffect:108 | P0 | onChange does setEmailFilter + setPage(1); emailFilter is a direct dependency of loadCustomers' useEffect, so every keystroke fires AdminService.adminListCustomers. Fast typing produces a burst of stale, racing requests with no cancellation. | Introduce a debouncedEmail value (300–400ms) and use ONLY debouncedEmail in the loadCustomers dependency list; keep emailFilter as the immediate controlled-input value so typing stays responsive. Add a useDebounce hook under lib/ (or useDeferredValue). Keep setPage(1) but tie the page reset to the debounced value so it doesn't thrash. No race-cancellation primitive exists, so debounce is the minimum fix. |
| Table row navigation (keyboard + semantics) | pages/customers.tsx:271-309 (TableRow onClick:276) | P1 | TableRow has onClick={() => router.push(...)} but NO tabIndex, role, or keydown handler — row navigation is completely keyboard-inaccessible (not merely missing a focus ring as two lenses assumed). The row also wraps an independent delete <button>, so the only keyboard-reachable element inside a 'clickable' row is Delete, with no way to reach the primary navigation. WCAG 2.1.1 (Keyboard) failure. | Remove onClick from TableRow. Make the email cell the navigation target: render the email as a real <a href={`/customers/${c.id}`}> (or Next <Link>) so it is natively focusable, keyboard-activatable, and right-click/open-in-new-tab capable. Keep the row hover/cursor cue for mouse users and add focus-within styling. This separates navigation (link) from the row's delete action (button) cleanly. Optionally add a chevron-right affordance in the email cell. |
| Create dialog form (labels, validation, submit) | pages/customers.tsx:351-403 (email 356, password 366, nickname 377, save 393) | P1 | Three Inputs have no id and their Labels have no htmlFor (WCAG 1.3.1 / 4.1.2 — screen readers can't name the fields). No required indicator / aria-required. Save's disabled prop only checks presence (!newEmail\|\|!newPassword), so 'a' passes as an email and the only feedback is a generic top-of-page error banner far from the field. Password Input lacks autocomplete='new-password'. The fields are not wrapped in a <form>, so Enter does not submit. | Wrap the three fields in <form onSubmit={e=>{e.preventDefault();handleCreate();}}> and make Save type='submit' so Enter works. Give each Input an id and each Label a matching htmlFor; mark email/password Label with a required asterisk + aria-required='true'. Add client-side email-format and password-min-length checks; on failure set aria-invalid='true' (Input already styles it) and render inline supporting text <p className='text-xs text-md-error' role='alert'> below the field instead of the banner. Add autocomplete='new-password' to the password field. autoFocus the email input on open. |
| Delete confirm dialog (loading + double-submit + buttons) | pages/customers.tsx:407-437 (handleDelete:128, delete btn:427) | P1 | handleDelete() is async but there is no in-flight state: the Delete button stays enabled, has no spinner, and can be clicked repeatedly firing multiple adminDeleteCustomer calls. Cancel is also not disabled mid-flight, creating an undefined race if clicked during deletion. The DialogContent description paragraph (415-417) is not linked via aria-describedby. | Add a `deleting` useState; set disabled={deleting} on BOTH buttons, show a spinner + '删除中…' on the destructive button during the call, and reset it in finally. Block Escape/overlay-close while deleting (guard onOpenChange). Add id='delete-dialog-desc' to the description <p> and aria-describedby='delete-dialog-desc' on DialogContent. Keep the existing email-in-message confirmation (sufficient for an admin context — name-typing confirmation is optional, not required here). |
| Delete row icon button (touch target) | pages/customers.tsx:296-306 | P1 | Hand-rolled icon button at size-8 (32×32px), below the M3 48dp / WCAG 2.5.8 tappable-target guidance, and bypasses the Button primitive's standardized focus/disabled behavior. Trash-only with aria-label but no tooltip. | Replace with <Button variant='ghost' size='icon' className='text-muted-foreground hover:text-md-error'> (icon = 40px) and wrap in the existing Tooltip ('删除客户') so the larger hit area + hover hint compensate for the icon-only affordance. If a true 48px target is required, add a size token rather than a one-off class. Keep e.stopPropagation() now that the row no longer owns onClick it's optional, but harmless. |
| Error banner (live region + dismiss) | pages/customers.tsx:213-219 | P1 | Dynamic error text conveyed by color + a dot, with no role='alert'/aria-live, so screen readers don't announce failures. Banner is also non-dismissible and persists after a later success. | Add role='alert' (assertive is appropriate for an operation failure) to the banner container. Add a trailing icon-Button (X, aria-label='关闭') that clears error state. Clear error automatically on the next successful load. For transient network errors a toast is preferable once a toast primitive exists (see below). |
| Refresh / Create header buttons (use primitive) | pages/customers.tsx:165-186 | P2 | Both are hand-rolled <button>s re-implementing state-layer/ripple/focus-ring/elevation that the Button primitive already standardizes; refresh is size-9 (36px). | Status filter Select (dead-code + value mapping) | pages/customers.tsx:93-94, 199-209 | P2 | Select maps sentinel '__all__' → '' on change, but loadCustomers checks `statusFilter !== 'all'` — 'all' is never produced, so that guard is dead code and the mapping is split across two conventions. #### pages/orders.tsx

- verdict: **major** · 控件数: 14 · P0/P1/P2: 1/2/11
- topPriority: 硬编码 limit:20、page:undefined、且完全忽略 API 已返回的 total——超过 20 条订单被静默截断且无任何提示与翻页入口。后端 adminListOrders 已支持 page 参数、handler_OrderListResponse 已含 total,纯属前端未接。这是系统状态可见性的直接违反,也是唯一的 P0。

| 控件 | 位置 | 严重度 | 反模式 | 重设计方案 |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Orders Table — 分页与 total | pages/orders.tsx:84-99 (loadOrders), 229-355 (Table) | P0 | loadOrders 写死 limit:20、page:undefined,且 setOrders 只取 data.items,完全丢弃 data.total。后端 adminListOrders 接受 page、handler_OrderListResponse 返回 total(已 grep 证实)。结果:订单>20 时静默截断,无总数、无页码、无上一页/下一页,用户无法发现其余数据。三份审查一致判定为本页最严重问题。 | ① 新增 page state(默认1)与 total state;loadOrders 传 page、读取 setTotal(data.total ?? 0)。② statusFilter 变化时重置 page=1。③ 在表格下方加服务端分页条:展示『第 (page-1)*20+1–min(page*20,total) 条,共 total 条』+ 上一页/下一页按钮(首/末页 disabled)。注意:components/ui/data-table.tsx 的分页是客户端的(getPaginationRowModel 对已加载 data 切片),不能用它解决服务端截断;此处需自建服务端分页条或仅复用其分页条 UI 外观。 |

#### pages/plans.tsx

- verdict: **major** · 控件数: 14 · P0/P1/P2: 1/3/10
- topPriority: handleDelete (lines 141-142) 的 catch 块完全为空：删除计划失败时用户零反馈，可能误以为删除成功而数据仍在，是本页最严重缺陷。必须先修。

| 控件 | 位置 | 严重度 | 反模式 | 重设计方案 |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| handleDelete — 删除失败静默吞错 | /home/kent/rk3528-hive/management/registry-ui/pages/plans.tsx:134-145 | P0 | async handleDelete 的 catch{} 块完全空白，删除请求失败后 finally 仍调用 setDeleting(false) 并关闭 dialog（实际未关，因为只有成功路径 setDeletePlan(null)），但无任何错误状态写入。破坏性操作失败完全无声，用户可能反复尝试或误判已删除。三视角一致判 major。 | 新增 deleteError 状态。catch (e) { setDeleteError(getErrorMessage(e, t('deleteFailed'))) }，在删除确认 Dialog 内（Save/Cancel 上方）以 bg-md-error-container 渲染错误，并加 role='alert'。失败时保持 dialog 打开，不调用 setDeletePlan(null)。loadPlans() 仅在成功分支调用（移出 finally），避免失败时悄悄刷新列表掩盖问题。openDelete/onClose 时清空 deleteError。 |
| Enabled/Disabled Toggle — 自定义 button 冒充 Switch | /home/kent/rk3528-hive/management/registry-ui/pages/plans.tsx:254-267 | P1 | 用 <button> + 圆点 + 文字手撸了一个 pill toggle 来表达启用/禁用二值开关，而项目已有 components/ui/switch.tsx（Radix Switch，含 role='switch'、aria-checked、键盘、focus ring）。当前实现虽是 <button>（空格可触发），但缺 role='switch' 与 aria-checked，屏幕阅读器无法播报开关状态。典型「换皮没换交互」。三视角一致判 major。 | 替换为 <Switch checked={formEnabled} onCheckedChange={setFormEnabled} id='plan-enabled' />，配 <Label htmlFor='plan-enabled'>{t('colStatus')}</Label>。废弃手写 button。状态色（启用 tertiary-container）已在表格行 badge 体现，dialog 内开关无需重复着色，交由 Switch 原语处理。 |
| 表格行操作 — Edit / Edit Lines / Delete 三按钮并排 | /home/kent/rk3528-hive/management/registry-ui/pages/plans.tsx:413-437 | P1 | 单行内塞 3 个文字按钮（含 destructive Delete），总宽 >150px，挤压表格、移动端易误触；且每个按钮 px-3 py-1.5（约 28px 高）低于 M3 触控目标。低优先级的 Edit Lines 与 destructive Delete 不应与主操作 Edit 平铺同权。 | 主操作 Edit 保留为行内 tonal 按钮但提高到 size 'sm'（h-8/py-2 起，达 ~40dp+）。Edit Lines + Delete 收进 DropdownMenu（'⋮' 图标触发，icon button 尺寸≥40dp）：菜单含「编辑线路」与「删除」，删除项用 destructive 文本色。这样行高更紧凑、destructive 不再裸露、触控目标达标。 |
| Create/Edit Dialog — 6 个数字输入无 NaN/越界校验 | /home/kent/rk3528-hive/management/registry-ui/pages/plans.tsx:219-249 | P1 | Traffic/Speed/Devices/Duration/Price/Sort Order 全是受控字符串 state，handleSave 直接 parseFloat/parseInt。用户清空或输入非法字符时 parseFloat 返回 NaN，Math.round(NaN*GB)=NaN 被静默 POST 给后端；Sort Order 连 min 都没有，可负可浮点。Lens A 判 major、Lens B 判 minor，仲裁为 P1：静默提交无效数据是真实数据完整性风险，而非纯 a11y 细节。 | handleSave 前做一次集中校验：对每个字段 const n = parseFloat(...); if (Number.isNaN(n) \|\| n < min) { setFormError(t('invalidInput')); return; }。Sort Order 补 min='0' step='1'，Speed/Devices/Duration 已是整数语义可加 step='1'。同时给每个 number Input 加 aria-invalid（校验失败时）。不强加业务上限（max=99 等），那是策略非 UX 缺陷。 |
| Lines Dialog — 原生 checkbox 而非 Checkbox 原语 | /home/kent/rk3528-hive/management/registry-ui/pages/plans.tsx:514-519 | P2 | 用 <input type='checkbox' className='accent-md-primary'> 包在 <label> 内。包裹关联本身有效（Lens B 判 ok），但缺设计系统统一的 focus-visible ring、disabled 态与 M3 视觉，和页面其它 Radix 控件不一致。 | 替换为 <Checkbox id={'line-'+l.id} checked={selectedLineIds.has(l.id!)} onCheckedChange={() => toggleLine(l.id!)} />，label 用 htmlFor 指向该 id（保留整行点击区）。可选：列表顶部加「已选 N 条」计数与全选/清空，提升多选可用性。 |
| 所有 Dialog Footer 按钮 — 原生 button 而非 Button 原语 | /home/kent/rk3528-hive/management/registry-ui/pages/plans.tsx:276-298,465-487,539-561 | P2 | Create/Edit、Delete、Lines 三个 dialog 的 Cancel/Save/Delete 全是手写 <button> + 长串 className（含 state-layer/ripple/elevation 重复拼接），与 components/ui/button.tsx 的 variant 体系并行维护，易漂移、尺寸/disabled 行为不统一。 | Cancel 用 <Button variant='outline'>，Save 用 <Button>（default/primary），Delete 用 <Button variant='destructive'>，loading 通过 disabled + 内嵌 spinner。删去重复 className。统一后顺带补 aria-disabled（Button 原语应已处理）。 |
