#### pages/portal/announcements.tsx

- verdict: **major** · 控件数: 15 · P0/P1/P2: 2/5/8
- topPriority: Error banner (lines 96-101) is a dead-end: no role="alert"/aria-live so screen readers never announce the fetch failure, and no Retry control so the only recovery is a manual full-page reload. Extract the loader, add role="alert", and add a Retry button — all three lenses rate this major.

| 控件 | 位置 | 严重度 | 反模式 | 重设计方案 |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Error banner — fetch-failure recovery + announcement | lines 96-101 (and loader at 56-73) | P0 | Persistent inline error container with no role="alert"/aria-live (SR never announces the failure on insert — WCAG 4.1.3), decorative AlertCircle not aria-hidden (adds noise), and ZERO recovery path: the only way out is a manual full-page reload (WCAG 3.3.4). It is neither a transient snackbar, a page-level error state, nor an actionable banner — M3-wise it matches no error pattern. | Extract the fetch into a reusable load() callback (so it can be re-invoked). Give the banner role="alert" aria-live="assertive". Mark AlertCircle aria-hidden="true". Add a Retry action (Button variant text/tonal, ≥48dp touch target on mobile) that re-runs load(); optionally a dismiss icon-button with aria-label. For a hard list-blocking failure, prefer a full-page error state (icon + message + filled 'Try again' + 'Back to dashboard' text button) instead of the thin banner. |
| Announcement title — semantic heading | lines 142-144 (CardTitle inner <span>) | P0 | Title is a visually-styled <span>, not a heading. With H1 only at page level, SR users cannot jump between announcements via heading navigation (NVDA/JAWS 'H' key), and the list has no per-item label — WCAG 1.3.1 (Info & Relationships) and 2.4.6 (Headings & Labels). Breaks on every card. | Render the title as <h2 id={`ann-${a.id}-title`} className="font-display text-base font-600 text-foreground">{a.title}</h2>. Keep the level icon + badges as siblings inside CardTitle (which stays a plain div). Reference the id from the card's aria-labelledby (see card-region change). |
| Card hover signifier on read-only items | lines 128-132; primitive at components/ui/card.tsx:10 | P1 | Card primitive hard-codes `transition-shadow ... hover:elevation-1`. These announcement cards have no onClick/role/tabindex/cursor, yet they raise on hover — a false affordance (Norman signifier error): users hover, see it lift, click, nothing happens. | Decouple interactivity from elevation in the primitive: gate the hover lift behind an `interactive` prop (or a data-attribute) so hover:elevation-1 only applies to genuinely clickable cards; non-interactive cards render flat. Apply the non-interactive variant here. Verify no regression on other pages that rely on the current hover lift. |
| Content body — HTML model, sanitizer config, links | lines 167-174 (dangerouslySetInnerHTML) | P1 | Sanitized HTML is injected into a <p>; DOMPurify legally allows block elements (ul/li/h*/pre) that a <p> cannot contain, so the browser auto-closes the <p> and fragments the DOM / reading order (WCAG 1.3.1). DOMPurify runs with default config (no explicit allow-list). Links get no target/rel and inherit color rather than the M3 link token. No length cap — a long critical notice and an old short one carry equal visual weight and balloon the page. | Switch the wrapper to a <div> so allowed block elements nest legally. Call DOMPurify.sanitize(html, { ALLOWED_TAGS:[...], ALLOWED_ATTR:[...,'target'] }) with an explicit white-list; post-process anchors to add target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" and style links with text-md-primary. Add an expand/collapse ('展开全文') above a threshold (~6 lines / 280 chars) so long content does not dominate. |
| Missing timestamp metadata | card body (no render of created_at/updated_at; data exists in model_Announcement) | P1 | created_at and updated_at exist on model_Announcement but are never shown. Customers cannot judge whether a critical/warning notice is fresh or stale — directly undercuts the credibility of urgent announcements and violates 'visibility of system status'. | Render a relative time near the title using <time dateTime={ISO}> (e.g. '3 小时前' / '昨天'), with the absolute timestamp exposed via title/Tooltip and aria-label. Localize via i18n. Feed it into the sort as a secondary key (see sort change). |
| Loading indicator — ARIA semantics + label | lines 104-112 | P1 | Indeterminate CSS spinner mislabeled role="progressbar" with no aria-valuenow/min/max — SR announces 'progressbar' then goes silent. The visible <p> reuses the page title (announcementsTitle), so SR users hear the title twice and get no 'loading' cue. Spinner div not aria-hidden. | Drop role="progressbar"; wrap the block with role="status" aria-live="polite" (or aria-busy on the list region) and aria-hidden the spinning div. Replace the <p> text with a dedicated key, e.g. t('loadingAnnouncements'), distinct from the H1; differentiate first-load vs refresh wording. |
| prefers-reduced-motion handling | lines 86,105,107,115,124,130-131 (animate-slide-up / animate-fade-in / animate-spin) | P1 | Multiple entrance animations plus a perpetual spinner run unconditionally; no prefers-reduced-motion respect (WCAG 2.3.3). Harms vestibular-sensitive users. | Either add a global @media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce) rule disabling .animate-spin/.animate-slide-up/.animate-fade-in, or switch usages to Tailwind motion-safe: variants. Apply project-wide via globals.css so all pages inherit it. |
| Level badge — use shared primitive + i18n + whitelist | lines 155-161 | P2 | Hand-rolled <span> chip reinvents the existing Badge primitive (which already has tonal variants + focus ring), and prints the raw API string a.level (critical/warning/info) — uppercase CSS is wasted in zh and an unexpected API value renders verbatim, breaking i18n. | Use <Badge variant={level==='critical' ? 'destructive' : level==='warning' ? 'secondary' : 'default'}> with a whitelist map (unknown → info + dev warning). Display t(`level.${level}`) instead of the raw string; drop uppercase in zh. |
| Pinned badge — use shared primitive | lines 146-153 | P2 | Pinned chip is another bespoke <span> duplicating Badge; Pin icon not aria-hidden and label is the bare word '置顶' rather than a full phrase. | Render via <Badge> for design-language consistency; aria-hidden the Pin icon and give the chip aria-label={t('pinnedAnnouncement')} so SR reads a complete phrase. |
| List + landmark semantics | lines 123 (list div), 84/86 (page root, no main/section), 128 (card has no region role) | P2 | List is a plain <div> (no <ul role="list">), so AT cannot count or jump to it; page body has no <main>/<section aria-labelledby> landmark; each Card lacks article/region role + aria-labelledby, so title, badges and content stream out flat with no per-item grouping. | Wrap the page in <main aria-labelledby="announcements-heading"> and give H1 that id. Render the list as <ul role="list" aria-label={t('announcementsTitle')}> with each card in an <li> (or article aria-labelledby={`ann-${a.id}-title`}). Optionally aria-live="polite" on the list so the loading→loaded swap is announced. |
| Empty state — semantics + next-best-action | lines 114-120 | P2 | Static empty block: Megaphone icon not aria-hidden, no role="status" (state change after a 0-result refresh is silent), and no CTA or context — first-time customers cannot tell 'system empty' from 'no access'. | aria-hidden the icon; wrap the message in role="status" aria-live="polite". Use context-aware copy ('暂无新公告，稍后再来看看') and optionally a tonal text button (Refresh / View plans / Contact support). |
| Search / filter / pagination | whole page | P2 | No search, level filter, or pagination. Beyond ~20 items the page grows unboundedly and customers cannot locate history or isolate critical notices (visibility of status / user control). | When count > ~10, add a debounced search Input (outlined text field) + level filter chips (M3 filter chips: All/critical/warning/info), or a 'recent N + load more' pattern. Sync query/level to URL (?q=&level=) for shareable/back-navigable state; collapse controls to a single ≥48dp row on mobile. |
| Sort — secondary ordering key | lines 75-81 | P2 | Sort is a single pinned-boolean comparison; within pinned and within non-pinned there is no order, so an old pinned notice can permanently sit above a newer critical one. | Add a stable secondary sort by created_at desc within each pinned group (now that the timestamp is surfaced), so newest pinned and newest critical float to the top of their groups. |
| Decorative icons missing aria-hidden | lines 88, 98, 117, 141, 150 | P2 | Megaphone (header + empty), AlertCircle (error), LevelIcon, and Pin are all decorative (paired text already conveys meaning) yet none carry aria-hidden="true", polluting SR output. | Add aria-hidden="true" to all five. Color is not the sole state carrier (text badges exist), so hiding the icons is safe and is a low-risk cleanup. |
| Data fetching — cancellation, deps, refresh | lines 56-73 | P2 | useEffect depends on the i18n t reference (re-fetches if t identity changes — fetch keyed on a translation fn is semantically wrong), cancellation is simulated with an `active` flag rather than AbortController, and there is no refresh entry point or new-announcement signal for long-lived sessions. | Key the effect on a stable trigger (mount + an explicit reload counter), read t inside without listing it as a fetch dependency. Use a real AbortController to cancel in-flight requests on unmount. Add a refresh icon-button by the H1 (and/or visibilitychange-based revalidate); on incremental data, surface a non-destructive 'new announcements' toast rather than silently swapping the list and losing scroll position. |

#### pages/portal/tickets.tsx

- verdict: **major** · 控件数: 16 · P0/P1/P2: 2/5/9
- topPriority: Two P0s: (1) header subtitle (line 158) renders the same i18n key as the h1 — a shipped content defect read twice by screen readers; (2) the New-Ticket create flow is keyboard/SR-inaccessible — fields are not in a <form>, Label↔Input are not programmatically associated, there is no Enter-to-submit and no required-field semantics. Both are low-effort, high-impact fixes that unblock the core action of the page.

| 控件 | 位置 | 严重度 | 反模式 | 重设计方案 |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Header subtitle <p> (duplicate title text) | pages/portal/tickets.tsx line 158 | P0 | The subtitle paragraph renders t('ticketsTitle'), identical to the h1 on line 157 — a copy-paste defect. Sighted users see the title twice; screen readers announce "工单 工单". | Introduce a distinct i18n key (e.g. ticketsSubtitle) describing the page ("查看与管理你的工单") and use it for the <p>. All three lenses flagged this independently; no conflict. |
| New-Ticket dialog form (Subject Input + Content Textarea + Submit) | pages/portal/tickets.tsx lines 284-337 | P0 | Fields are bare divs, not wrapped in <form>; Label (286,295) has no htmlFor and Input/Textarea (287,296) have no id, so SR users hear no field name (placeholder is not a label, WCAG 3.3.2/1.3.1); submit is an onClick button with no type, so Enter never submits; no aria-required and the silent disabled state gives no reason the button is inert. | Wrap both fields in <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>; give Input id="new-subject" + Label htmlFor, Textarea id="new-content" + Label htmlFor; add aria-required="true" and a visible required marker; make submit type="submit" with aria-busy={submitting}; keep disabled guard but add aria-describedby pointing at a hint. Arbitration: Lens B/C suggested 'keep always enabled + inline validation' — defer that as taste; the required fix is association + form + type. This single change resolves the most issues at once. |
| Clickable ticket rows (navigate to detail) | pages/portal/tickets.tsx lines 246-268 | P1 | <tr> uses cursor-pointer + tabIndex={0} + onClick + onKeyDown Enter-only, with no role and no aria-label, so SR users hear only cell text (not that it navigates) and keyboard users can't activate with Space; focus is shown only via focus-visible:bg-md-surface-container-high (background tint), which likely fails WCAG 2.4.7 visible-focus contrast. | Add role="link" and aria-label (e.g. `查看工单 #${id}: ${subject}`); handle both Enter and Space in onKeyDown; replace background-only focus with a real ring/outline (focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-md-primary). Add a trailing chevron-right cell as a visual affordance. All three lenses agree. |
| List error banner + dialog submit-error banner | pages/portal/tickets.tsx lines 194-200 and 305-311 | P1 | Neither banner has role="alert"/aria-live, so load and submit failures are silent to screen readers; the list banner also offers no inline remediation — the user must hunt for the header Refresh button. | Add role="alert" (or aria-live="assertive") to both banners; add an inline "重试" button to the list banner that calls loadTickets; mark the AlertCircle icons aria-hidden. |
| Reply textarea (detail page) | pages/portal/tickets/[id].tsx lines 173-182 | P1 | The textarea has only a placeholder, no <Label> or aria-label, so SR users hear no field name. (Ctrl/Cmd+Enter submit is already correctly implemented.) | Add a visible <Label htmlFor> or aria-label ("回复内容"). Keep the existing keyboard shortcut. |
| Reply submit button loading feedback (detail page) | pages/portal/tickets/[id].tsx lines 190-202 | P1 | During send the label swaps to 'saving' but no spinner appears (only the static Send icon), inconsistent with the create dialog which shows CircularProgress; no aria-busy. | Swap the Send icon for a CircularProgress while sending and add aria-busy={sending}, matching the dialog's pattern. |
| Header buttons (New Ticket / Refresh) and dialog footer buttons (Cancel / Submit) | pages/portal/tickets.tsx lines 164-189, 316-337 | P1 | These are hand-rolled <button> elements duplicating button styling inline instead of using the Button primitive; py-2 yields ~36-40px height, below the M3 48dp touch minimum the design contract mandates; none declare type, and decorative Plus/RefreshCw icons aren't aria-hidden. | Migrate to the Button primitive (centralizes sizing, focus, type, ripple) and ensure the rendered height is >=48dp on touch (e.g. h-11/h-12); add type="button" to non-submit actions; mark decorative icons aria-hidden. Arbitration: Lens C's 'convert primary to FAB' is rejected — the header button group is the app-wide established pattern post-redesign; only the sizing/semantics need fixing. |
| Subject input autoFocus on dialog open | pages/portal/tickets.tsx lines 287-292 | P2 | When the dialog opens, focus is not placed on the first field, so keyboard users must Tab into it. | Add autoFocus to the Subject input (Radix Dialog already manages the focus trap, so this just sets the initial target). |
| Empty state (no tickets) | pages/portal/tickets.tsx lines 232-243 | P2 | Shows an inbox icon + '暂无工单' with no call-to-action; a first-time user on an empty support inbox has no path to create a ticket from this state. InboxIcon not aria-hidden, container has no role=status. | Add a primary '创建第一个工单' button that opens the same dialog; mark the icon aria-hidden and add role="status" to the container. |
| Table column headers (a11y association) | pages/portal/tickets.tsx lines 207-218 via components/ui/table.tsx | P2 | TableHead renders a plain <th> with no scope="col", weakening header/data association for screen readers (WCAG 1.3.1). | Add scope="col" to the TableHead primitive so every table in the app benefits. |
| Page animations (fade-in / slide-up / scale-in / spin) | pages/portal/tickets.tsx page-wide (and globals.css) | P2 | Multiple entrance animations run unconditionally with no prefers-reduced-motion guard (WCAG 2.3.3), affecting users with vestibular sensitivity. | Add a global @media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce) rule in globals.css that neutralizes animation/transition durations, or apply Tailwind motion-reduce: variants. Not a components/ui primitive — fix in globals.css. |
| Ticket list data fetch (pagination metadata discarded) | pages/portal/tickets.tsx lines 91-96 | P2 | portalTickets({}) returns a paginated payload but the code keeps only data.items and drops page metadata; there is no page size, next/prev, or 'showing N of M' — the list silently truncates or over-fetches as a customer accumulates tickets. | Pass page/pageSize params and render a pager (or 'load more') plus a count label using the returned metadata. Arbitration: full search/sort (below) is optional for a single customer's own list, but honoring the API's existing pagination is concrete and should be done. |
| Subject / Content length feedback | pages/portal/tickets.tsx lines 287-302 | P2 | No maxLength or character counter; if the backend enforces a limit the user only learns via a post-submit server error. | If the backend enforces limits, add maxLength plus a small 'n/max' counter under each field; otherwise omit. |
| Post-create success feedback | pages/portal/tickets.tsx lines 124-127 | P2 | On success the dialog closes and the whole list reloads synchronously with no confirmation, so the user may not realize the ticket was created. | Show a snackbar/toast ('工单已创建') after close; consider optimistic insertion of the new row so it appears immediately instead of after a blocking reload. |
| Dialog dismissal with unsaved input | pages/portal/tickets.tsx lines 276, 316-324 | P2 | Esc, overlay-click, the X, and Cancel all discard typed Subject/Content silently with no confirmation. | Acceptable for this 2-field form today; if non-empty, intercept onEscapeKeyDown/onOpenChange to confirm '放弃工单?'. Low priority until the form grows. |
| List query controls (search / status filter / sort) | pages/portal/tickets.tsx (absent; header lines 151-191, table 204-218) | P2 | No search box, no status filter chips (open/replied/closed), no column sort; Lens A and C rated this 'major'. | Arbitration: downgraded to P2. This is a customer viewing only their own tickets, where counts are typically small; the higher-value scalability fix is pagination (above). If/when lists grow, add a status filter-chip row (reusing the existing chip styling) and click-to-sort headers with aria-sort. Make StatusChip optionally clickable to drive the filter. |

#### pages/portal/tickets/[id].tsx

- verdict: **major** · 控件数: 14 · P0/P1/P2: 1/5/8
- topPriority: 替换发送按钮为 Button 原语（default variant）——这是页面主操作，却用手搓 state-layer/elevation 类完全旁路了设计系统契约，是本页最典型的「换皮没换交互」违规，且 Button(line 9) 已 import 仅未使用。

| 控件 | 位置 | 严重度 | 反模式 | 重设计方案 |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| 发送回复按钮 (Send) | lines 190-202 | P0 | 页面主操作用裸 <button> + 手搓 state-layer/ripple/elevation-1/disabled:opacity-38 类，完全复刻 Button 的 default variant 却旁路 CVA/Slot/统一 focus 环。注意 opacity-38 与系统 disabled:opacity-40 不一致，且 Button 在 line 9 已 import 但未使用——三审一致判 major。 | 整体替换为 <Button onClick={handleReply} disabled={sending \|\| !replyContent.trim()}><Send className="h-4 w-4" aria-hidden="true" />{sending ? tCommon('saving') : t('reply')}</Button>，删除全部手搓类。default variant 自带 elevation-1/hover:elevation-2 与 disabled:opacity-40，行为完全等价。 |
| 回复 Textarea 缺少程序化标签 | lines 173-182 | P1 | 仅靠 placeholder 提供语义，无 <label>/aria-label，违反 WCAG 3.3.2 与 4.1.2；低视力用户聚焦后 placeholder 消失即失去上下文。同时 sendError 存在时未联动 aria-invalid / aria-describedby。 | 加视觉隐藏 label：<label htmlFor="reply-content" className="sr-only">{t('reply')}</label>，Textarea 加 id="reply-content"、aria-invalid={!!sendError}、aria-describedby={sendError ? 'reply-error' : undefined}。Textarea 原语已支持 aria-invalid 样式透传，无需改原语。注意：styles/globals.css 当前无 .sr-only 工具类，需确认 Tailwind 内置 sr-only 是否启用，否则补一条。 |
| 发送后无成功反馈 | lines 69-85 (handleReply) | P1 | 回复成功后仅静默 loadTicket() 重载，无任何确认（Nielsen+M3 双审判 major）。用户可能误以为未发送而重复提交。仓库无 toast/Snackbar/sonner 原语，故不强行引入新框架。 | 新增 sentOk 瞬时状态：发送成功后置 true 并 setTimeout 3s 清除，渲染 <span role="status" aria-live="polite"> 的内联确认条（如「回复已发送」），复用 bg-md-primary-container/text-md-on-primary-container。同时兼顾屏幕阅读器播报与可见反馈。 |
| 返回按钮 (Back) | lines 109-118 | P1 | 裸 <button> + 手搓 bg-md-primary-container 类旁路 Button；用 router.push 命令式跳转而非 Link，丢失 Next.js prefetch 与浏览器前进/后退语义。 | 替换为 <Button variant="secondary" size="sm" asChild><Link href="/portal/tickets"><ArrowLeft className="h-4 w-4" aria-hidden="true" /><span>{tCommon('back')}</span></Link></Button>。secondary variant 即 secondary-container 等价当前配色。 |
| 工单关闭态：表单静默隐藏无去向 | lines 170-206 (isClosed 分支) | P1 | isClosed 时仅用 {!isClosed && ...} 隐藏整个回复表单，无任何说明或出口，用户不知能否重开或如何继续求助。注意：仲裁驳回 M3 审的「加关闭/重开按钮」——后端只有 adminCloseTicket，无 portalCloseTicket，门户客户无对应 API。 | isClosed 时渲染关闭横幅替代空白：用 bg-md-surface-container-high 卡片显示「此工单已关闭」+ <Button variant="default" asChild><Link href="/portal/tickets/new">提交新工单</Link></Button>。此方案不依赖新后端接口。客户自助关闭/重开需新增门户 API，单列为后端待办、不在本页前端范围。 |
| 错误消息未被辅助技术播报（sendError + 加载错误） | lines 94-99 (load error), 183-188 (send error) | P1 | 两处动态错误均用普通 <p>/<div>，无 role="alert"/aria-live，违反 WCAG 4.1.3；屏幕阅读器用户感知不到失败。装饰性圆点也未 aria-hidden。 | load error 容器加 role="alert"；send error 段落加 id="reply-error" role="alert" aria-live="assertive"（与 Textarea 的 aria-describedby 配对）。两处圆点 span 加 aria-hidden="true"。 |
| 发送后整页 spinner 闪烁 | lines 41-53 (loadTicket setLoading), lines 88-93 | P2 | handleReply 成功后调用 loadTicket() 会 setLoading(true)，触发整页 spinner 重挂载，对话区瞬间清空再重绘，体验割裂。 | 拆分 refreshing 状态：发送后的重取不走整页 loading 分支，改为局部细指示（如发送条上的轻量进度）或乐观更新——成功后先把新回复 append 到本地 ticket.replies，再后台静默 refetch 校准。 |
| 自动滚动忽略用户阅读位置 | lines 60-62 | P2 | 每当 replies.length 变化即 scrollIntoView 强制滚到底，含初次加载（跳过历史）与管理员新回复（打断正在上翻历史的用户）。 | 仅当用户已接近底部（距底 <100px）时才自动滚动；初次加载不滚动（用 ref 标记首渲染）。上翻时若有新消息，显示「新消息」回到底部小药丸（可选）。 |
| 加载错误态缺重试与返回出口 | lines 94-99 | P2 | 错误页只有一行文字，无重试按钮也无返回列表入口，用户被困需手动刷新。 | 在错误容器内加 <Button variant="outline" size="sm" onClick={loadTicket}>{tCommon('retry')}</Button> 与 <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" asChild><Link href="/portal/tickets">{tCommon('back')}</Link></Button>。 |
| 工单元信息缺失（创建/更新时间） | lines 120-125 (header) | P2 | 头部仅 #id + subject + 状态，缺创建/最后更新时间，用户无法判断工单时效。仲裁修正 M3 审：model_Ticket 无 priority/category 字段，故只补 created_at/updated_at，不臆造优先级/分类。 | 标题下加一行 text-xs text-muted-foreground 元信息：formatDate(tk.created_at) 创建、tk.updated_at 更新。仅用 API 已有字段。 |
| 装饰性图标缺 aria-hidden | lines 90 (spinner), 116 (ArrowLeft), 138 (MessageCircle), 200 (Send) | P2 | spinner span 与 ArrowLeft/MessageCircle/Send 图标均未 aria-hidden，旁有可见文字时屏幕阅读器读出冗余图标名（如「发送 发送」）。 | 全部图标/spinner 加 aria-hidden="true"。文字已作为 accessible name。 |
| 对话容器无动态区域语义 | lines 134-167 | P2 | 回复线程容器是裸 div，新回复到达不被屏幕阅读器播报；移动端 max-w-[75%] 气泡可能贴边（容器无横向 padding）。 | 容器加 role="log" aria-live="polite"；窄屏加 px-1 sm:px-0 或减小气泡 max-w（如 max-w-[85%] sm:max-w-[75%]）防贴边。 |
| Ctrl/Cmd+Enter 快捷键提示输入后消失 | lines 174,179-181 | P2 | 仲裁修正 M3/Nielsen 审：快捷键提示其实已在 placeholder（zh.json:434「输入回复内容…（Ctrl+Enter 发送）」），并非完全不可见；但 placeholder 在输入后即消失，power user 输入中无持久提示。 | 把快捷键提示从 placeholder 移到发送按钮旁的常驻 text-xs text-muted-foreground，或 Tooltip 包裹 Send 按钮显示「Ctrl+Enter」。placeholder 保留纯引导文案。 |
| 回复输入无字数上限/计数 | lines 173-182 | P2 | Textarea 无 maxLength 与实时计数，存在服务端截断风险且用户无感知。 | 确认后端 content 长度上限后加 maxLength 与 0/N 实时计数（aria-live="polite"）。需先核对后端约束再定上限值。 |


## 4. P0 全局清单

> 所有 P0（最高优先级）改动汇总。`来源` 标注所属页面 / 原语。

| 来源 | 控件 | 位置 | 反模式 | 重设计方案 |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `pages/dashboard.tsx` | Dashboard 数据加载缺 error state(silent failure) | pages/dashboard.tsx:90-94 | sessionApi(AdminService.nodesList({})).then(setNodes).finally(setLoading(false)) 无 .catch。API 失败时 nodes 保持 [],loading=false,页面渲染 0 total / 0 online / 0 offline + 空表,与「真实空机群」视觉完全一致。管理员无法区分『后端宕机』与『确实没有节点』,造成根本性运维误判。三份审查一致标为最高优先级。 | 加 const [error, setError] = useState<unknown>(null);在 useEffect 内 .catch((e) => setError(e))。渲染顺序:loading → skeleton;!loading && error → 错误态(AlertTriangle 图标 + 文案『无法加载机群数据』+ <Button onClick={refetch}>重试</Button>,把 fetch 抽成可复用的 loadNodes 函数供重试调用);!loading && !error → 正常内容。错误文案走 i18n。 |
| `pages/nodes.tsx` | 单行 Delete 菜单项 | nodes.tsx:166 (handleDelete) + 250-254 (DropdownMenuItem) | 破坏性删除走原生 window.confirm()。该弹窗不 trap 焦点、无 aria-describedby 说明后果、dark mode 下样式失控、与 Radix 键盘行为不一致；确认仅靠 i18n 文案，无二次校验。 | 改为 role=alertdialog 的 Dialog：标题=删除节点，正文带 error 图标 + 明确列出 mac/hostname + 不可逆提示，焦点默认落在 Cancel，确认按钮用 destructive variant。删除成功/失败用 aria-live 内联反馈。 |
| `pages/nodes.tsx` | 批量删除按钮 + batchAction('delete') | nodes.tsx:175-184 (batchAction) + 410-417 (Button) | 三连缺陷：(1) 原生 confirm() 仅显示数量、不列具体节点；(2) for...of 串行 await，N 个节点等待时间线性增长且无进度；(3) .catch(()=>{}) 静默吞错，部分失败时用户完全无感知。 | Dialog 确认时列出前 5 个节点名/MAC +「等 N 个」与不可逆警告；执行改 Promise.allSettled 并发（限并发≈5）；收集失败项，完成后用 aria-live 内联横幅回报「成功 X、失败 Y：mac1, mac2」；处理中 disable 批量条按钮并显示进度。 |
| `pages/nodes/detail.tsx` | enabled 启用/禁用 Select | line 263-271 | 布尔二元量用 Select dropdown 承载，需 展开→点击→关闭 三步切换；且两个 SelectItem 文案完全相同（'✓ 启用' / '✗ 启用'，line 267-268），仅图标区分，用户与屏幕阅读器都无法从文字判断哪项是关。底层值 '1'/'0' 经 SelectValue 朗读也非语义化。三份审查一致 major。 | 替换为 Switch：<div class="flex items-center gap-3"><Switch id="detail-enabled" checked={enabled} onCheckedChange={setEnabled} /><Label htmlFor="detail-enabled">{t('enabled')}</Label></div>。单击切换，Radix Switch 自带 role="switch"+aria-checked。移除歧义文案。 |
| `pages/gateway.tsx` | Feedback Snackbar (success/error status div) | gateway.tsx:243-259 | 三视角一致判 major。该状态条既不可关闭、也不自动消失——一旦出现会持续到下一次 patchField 才被 setFeedback(null) 覆盖,过时消息可滞留整个 session。更严重的是它只是个带样式的 <div>,无 role / aria-live,屏幕阅读器在保存成功或失败时完全无播报。这违背 transient feedback 最佳实践和 WCAG 4.1.3 Status Messages。 | 重构为真正的 Snackbar 行为:(1) useEffect 监听 feedback,setTimeout 4000ms 后 setFeedback(null),return 清理 timer(成功态自动消失;错误态可延长或保留)。(2) 错误态加一个 X 关闭图标按钮(用 Button size="icon-xs" variant="ghost")。(3) 容器加 role={feedback.kind==='err' ? 'alert' : 'status'} 与 aria-live={feedback.kind==='err' ? 'assertive' : 'polite'} aria-atomic="true"。建议长期抽成共享 Snackbar/Toast 原语,因为该模式在多页复用。 |

| `pages/portal/tickets.tsx` | New-Ticket dialog form (Subject Input + Content Textarea + Submit) | pages/portal/tickets.tsx lines 284-337 | Fields are bare divs, not wrapped in <form>; Label (286,295) has no htmlFor and Input/Textarea (287,296) have no id, so SR users hear no field name (placeholder is not a label, WCAG 3.3.2/1.3.1); submit is an onClick button with no type, so Enter never submits; no aria-required and the silent disabled state gives no reason the button is inert. | Wrap both fields in <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>; give Input id="new-subject" + Label htmlFor, Textarea id="new-content" + Label htmlFor; add aria-required="true" and a visible required marker; make submit type="submit" with aria-busy={submitting}; keep disabled guard but add aria-describedby pointing at a hint. Arbitration: Lens B/C suggested 'keep always enabled + inline validation' — defer that as taste; the required fix is association + form + type. This single change resolves the most issues at once. |
| `pages/portal/tickets/[id].tsx` | 发送回复按钮 (Send) | lines 190-202 | 页面主操作用裸 <button> + 手搓 state-layer/ripple/elevation-1/disabled:opacity-38 类，完全复刻 Button 的 default variant 却旁路 CVA/Slot/统一 focus 环。注意 opacity-38 与系统 disabled:opacity-40 不一致，且 Button 在 line 9 已 import 但未使用——三审一致判 major。 | 整体替换为 <Button onClick={handleReply} disabled={sending \|\| !replyContent.trim()}><Send className="h-4 w-4" aria-hidden="true" />{sending ? tCommon('saving') : t('reply')}</Button>，删除全部手搓类。default variant 自带 elevation-1/hover:elevation-2 与 disabled:opacity-40，行为完全等价。 |
| `components/ui/data-table.tsx` | Sortable column header (TableHead with onClick sort) | data-table.tsx:229-243 | Sort is wired via onClick on the <th> with cursor-pointer/hover styling, but there is no tabIndex, no role=button, no onKeyDown (Enter/Space), and no aria-sort attribute. Keyboard users cannot trigger a sort at all, and screen readers never announce that a column is sortable or its current asc/desc state — the ArrowUp/Down icons are decorative and uncommunicated. This is a hard a11y blocker inherited by every caller. | Wrap the header label+icon in a real <button type=button> (sort is an action, not a cell) so it is natively focusable and keyboard-activatable, OR add tabIndex=0 + role=button + onKeyDown handling Enter/Space to call getToggleSortingHandler(). Set aria-sort on the <th> to 'ascending'/'descending'/'none' from getIsSorted(). Give the sort control an aria-label like `Sort by {columnLabel}`. Mark the arrow icons aria-hidden. Add focus-visible ring matching the M3 token already used elsewhere. |
| `components/ui/data-table.tsx` | Clickable row (onRowClick on <tr>) | data-table.tsx:264-271 | Row navigation is onClick on a <tr> with cursor-pointer but no tabIndex, no role, no keyboard handler, and no accessible name. In nodes.tsx this row click is the primary way to open node detail, so the whole drill-down is mouse-only and invisible to AT. Worse, stopPropagation is keyed off hardcoded column ids ('__select','actions') at line 273 — any other interactive content placed in a cell (a link, a Switch, a menu) will swallow into row navigation, a silent footgun for every future caller. | Prefer making the navigable cell content a real link/button (semantic, mid-table accessible) rather than a clickable row. If row-level click must stay, add role=button + tabIndex=0 + onKeyDown(Enter/Space) + an aria-label describing the destination, and a focus-visible ring. Replace the hardcoded interactive-column list with an explicit per-column flag (e.g. column.meta.stopRowClick) so callers opt in rather than relying on magic ids. |
| `components/ui/dialog.tsx` | AlertDialog / destructive-confirm variant | dialog.tsx — entire file (no alertdialog export); callers e.g. pages/plans.tsx:454-489, customers/[id].tsx, orders.tsx, users.tsx, lines.tsx | There is no AlertDialog primitive. Every destructive confirmation reuses the generic Dialog, so the dialog announces as role="dialog" not role="alertdialog", does not force initial focus onto the safe (Cancel) action, and each page re-implements an inline animate-spin SVG + bg-md-error button + `disabled={deleting}` (plans.tsx:475-486 duplicated verbatim across ~6 pages). Confirmation semantics, focus order, and busy state are decided per-caller instead of by the shared control. | Export AlertDialog/AlertDialogContent/AlertDialogAction/AlertDialogCancel wrapping radix-ui AlertDialog (role=alertdialog, focus defaults to Cancel). Give AlertDialogAction a `loading` boolean that renders the shared Spinner, sets aria-busy, and disables the button; and a `destructive` style hook mapping to bg-md-error/md-on-error. This removes the copy-pasted SVG and standardizes confirm UX. |
| `components/ui/dialog.tsx` | DialogContent — pending/async dismissal guard | dialog.tsx:50-82 | DialogContent forwards no controlled props for dismissal, so while an async delete/save is in flight (`deleting`/`saving` true) the user can still press Escape or click the overlay and dismiss the dialog — the request keeps running but the UI unmounts, orphaning the spinner/feedback and risking a state desync. The X close button also stays interactive during pending state. | Add a `dismissible`/`pending` prop on DialogContent that, when pending, wires onEscapeKeyDown/onPointerDownOutside/onInteractOutside to preventDefault and disables the close button. Default keeps current behavior; destructive/submit flows pass pending to lock the surface until the operation resolves. |
| `components/ui/dialog.tsx` | DialogDescription wiring (aria-describedby) | dialog.tsx:50-82 (Content) & 134-145 (Description); 22 DialogContent usages, 0 DialogDescription usages in pages/ | DialogDescription is exported but used 0 times across all 22 DialogContent call sites, and DialogContent neither renders a description slot nor passes `aria-describedby={undefined}`. Radix therefore emits a runtime a11y warning for every dialog and, more importantly, screen-reader users get a title with no described context for the dialog body. Body copy is placed in raw <p> tags (plans.tsx:460) that are never associated to the dialog. | Either (a) accept an optional `description` prop on DialogContent that renders a DialogDescription with a generated id and sets aria-describedby, or (b) pass aria-describedby={undefined} explicitly when no description is provided to suppress the warning. Update call sites to pass real description text so confirmation/forms are announced. |
| `components/ui/command.tsx` | CommandDialog | components/ui/command.tsx:43-58 | DialogHeader (containing the sr-only DialogTitle + DialogDescription) is rendered as a SIBLING before DialogContent, not as a descendant of it. Radix Dialog wires aria-labelledby/aria-describedby by locating DialogTitle/Description INSIDE the content node. As written the content has no Title descendant: the modal opens with no accessible name, screen readers announce only 'dialog', and Radix emits its console warning 'DialogContent requires a DialogTitle'. Every consumer of this palette inherits the defect. | Move the DialogHeader (sr-only Title/Description) INSIDE DialogContent, above the Command. Keep it visually hidden but in the accessibility tree. Confirm Radix no longer warns. Optionally expose aria-describedby wiring so the description is announced. |
| `components/ui/dropdown-menu.tsx` | DropdownMenuItem / CheckboxItem / RadioItem / SubTrigger — touch target height | dropdown-menu.tsx:75 (Item), :93 (Checkbox), :129 (Radio), :212 (SubTrigger) | All four interactive item types use `px-2.5 py-2 text-sm` → 8px top/bottom padding + ~20px line-height ≈ 36px row height. M3 mandates ≥48dp pointer targets. On nodes.tsx the dropdown holds View + Delete (destructive) actions hit by finger on mobile; data-table column-toggle checkboxes are even smaller-feeling because the indicator sits in a 14px box. No way for a consumer to opt into a comfortable size. | Add a `size?: 'sm' \| 'default' \| 'comfortable'` prop (or a CVA variant) to the item family. `comfortable` (mobile default) → `min-h-12 py-2.5`; `default` (dense desktop menus) → `min-h-9`. Set the family default to enforce `min-h-9` at minimum and `min-h-12` under a coarse-pointer media query (`pointer-coarse:min-h-12`). Apply identically to CheckboxItem/RadioItem/SubTrigger so checked-state and submenu rows match. |
| `components/ui/dropdown-menu.tsx` | DropdownMenuItem — destructive confirmation semantics | dropdown-menu.tsx:60-81 + consumer pages/nodes.tsx:165 (window.confirm) / :251 delete item | The primitive exposes `variant="destructive"` purely as a color token; it carries no interaction contract. The only consumer wires destructive delete to a native `window.confirm()` (nodes.tsx:166,178). A destructive menu item that fires immediately on select/Enter with only a browser-native confirm is inconsistent with the app's own Dialog primitive and is easy for other consumers to copy without any confirm at all. Nothing in the primitive nudges callers toward a guarded flow. | Keep `variant="destructive"` for styling but document/enforce a guarded pattern: either expose a `confirm?: { title; description; confirmLabel }` prop that internally renders the AlertDialog/Dialog primitive on select (preventing default close), or ship a `DropdownMenuDestructiveItem` wrapper that requires a confirm handler. At minimum, destructive items should not auto-dismiss the menu before confirmation resolves. Replace window.confirm usage in nodes.tsx with the dialog primitive. |
| `components/ui/location-combobox.tsx` | 外部 Label 无法关联触发器（无障碍断链） | location-combobox.tsx:35-46 + 调用方 detail.tsx:245 | 调用方用 <Label>{t('location')}</Label> 但触发器是 role=combobox 的 Button，既无 id 也不接受 aria-labelledby/aria-label。Label 没有 htmlFor，点击 Label 不聚焦控件，屏幕阅读器朗读时只报 'combobox 折叠'，读不出字段名 '地区'。所有调用方都复刻这个断链。 | 新增 id?: string 与 ariaLabelledby?: string（或 'aria-label'）prop。把 id 透传到触发 Button，调用方 Label 用 htmlFor 指向它；或让控件内部用 aria-labelledby 关联外部 label id。补充 aria-haspopup="listbox"。 |
| `components/ui/checkbox.tsx` | Checkbox 触控目标尺寸 | components/ui/checkbox.tsx:14-15 (size-[18px]) | 复选框可点区域被硬定为 size-[18px](18dp),没有任何不可见命中区(::before/伪元素)扩展。M3 规范要求所有交互控件触控目标 ≥48dp。data-table 的行/全选列与 gateway 弹层里 Checkbox 直接裸用,移动端 18dp 的命中区几乎不可能精准点中,且相邻行复选框间距过小易误触。视觉上保持 18dp 没问题,但命中区必须独立放大。 | 视觉方块保持 18dp 不变,新增一个不可见的 48x48 命中层:在 Root 上加 before 伪元素 'before:absolute before:left-1/2 before:top-1/2 before:size-12 before:-translate-x-1/2 before:-translate-y-1/2 before:content-[""]',并把 Root 设为 relative(已是 relative)。或暴露 size 变体('sm'=20dp 视觉/'md'=24dp)同时命中区恒为 48dp。确保命中层不影响 flex 布局(伪元素 absolute 不占位)。 |
| `components/ui/checkbox.tsx` | indeterminate(半选)状态语义 | components/ui/checkbox.tsx:25-30; 调用方 data-table.tsx:108-112 | Indicator 内永远渲染 CheckIcon,完全没处理 Radix 原生支持的 checked="indeterminate"。data-table 的全选表头用的是 getIsAllPageRowsSelected()(布尔),当本页只选中部分行时,标准 M3/桌面交互应显示横线(–)的半选态,这里无法表达——用户看到全选框是「未勾」,但实际已选若干行,反馈与真实状态不符,且 ARIA 也不会播报 mixed。 | 在 Indicator 内按状态切换图标:data-[state=indeterminate] 显示 MinusIcon,data-[state=checked] 显示 CheckIcon(可用两个带 data-state 条件 class 的 Indicator,或读 props.checked 决定)。同步把 data-table 全选 checked 改为 'all \| indeterminate(部分) \| false',onCheckedChange 配合 toggleAllPageRowsSelected。Radix 会自动把 aria-checked 设为 'mixed',无障碍随之正确。 |
| `components/ui/input.tsx` | Input root — fixed height | components/ui/input.tsx:11 ("h-10 ...") | Height is locked to h-10 (40px) with no size prop. M3 spec and the review brief require touch targets >= 48dp. Every caller (login, portal forms, users/customers/plans dialogs, and the data-table search field at data-table.tsx:169) inherits a 40px hit area, so the violation is fleet-wide and unfixable from call sites without className hacks. | Add a size variant via cva: size='md' (default, h-12 / 48px to satisfy M3 touch), size='sm' (h-10, opt-in for dense desktop tables only). Keep text-base on mobile (prevents iOS zoom), md:text-sm on >=md. Density-sensitive callers like data-table can pass size='sm' explicitly; default path is spec-compliant. |
| `components/layout/Sidebar.tsx` | Sidebar container (whole aside) — responsive strategy | Sidebar.tsx:68 (aside w-60 shrink-0) + AppLayout.tsx:42 (renders <Sidebar/> unconditionally) | aside is 'flex h-screen w-60 shrink-0' with no breakpoint prefixes; AppLayout places it as a permanent flex column. There is no hamburger trigger, no off-canvas drawer, no overlay, no md:/lg: hiding anywhere in the repo.
